## Biblical Prophecy: Daniel and Revelation - The Beast System

**Both Daniel and Revelation describe the same prophetic beast system** - a power that would arise from the fourth kingdom (Rome), persecute God's people, change His law, and enforce false worship. Daniel provides the historical framework; Revelation expands with additional details about the final conflict. Together, they form a complete picture of the Sabbath change and the coming test of loyalty.

---

### **Understanding Biblical Symbols: Key to Prophecy**

Before examining Daniel and Revelation's prophecies, it's essential to understand the symbolic language the Bible uses. Scripture interprets its own symbols - we don't need to guess their meaning.

#### **Prophetic Symbols Explained by Scripture**

| **Symbol** | **Meaning** | **Biblical Reference** |
|-----------|------------|---------------------|
| **Beast** | Kingdom/Nation/Political Power | Daniel 7:17, 23: "These great beasts... are four **kings**... The fourth beast shall be the fourth **kingdom**" |
| **Waters/Sea** | Peoples/Nations/Multitudes/Languages | Revelation 17:15: "The waters... are **peoples, multitudes, nations, and tongues**" |
| **Earth/Land** | Sparsely populated area, established territory | Contrast to "sea" (densely populated, turbulent masses) |
| **Horns** | Kings/Powers/Kingdoms | Daniel 7:24: "The ten horns are **ten kings**"; Revelation 17:12 |
| **Heads** | Kings/Rulers/Governments | Revelation 17:9-10: "The seven heads are seven mountains... **seven kings**" |
| **Woman (pure)** | True Church (God's faithful people) | Revelation 12:1: Woman clothed with sun (righteousness) |
| **Woman (harlot)** | Apostate Church (unfaithful to God) | Revelation 17:1-5: Great harlot, "BABYLON THE GREAT" |
| **Wings** | Speed of conquest | Daniel 7:4, 6: Lion with eagle's wings, leopard with 4 wings |
| **Little Horn** | Religious-political power arising among kingdoms | Daniel 7:8, 24-25: Rose among ten horns, different from others |
| **Dragon** | Satan/Evil power | Revelation 12:9: "The great dragon... that serpent of old, called the **Devil and Satan**" |
| **Lamb** | Jesus Christ (true Lamb); or deceptive appearance (false lamb) | John 1:29: "Behold! The **Lamb of God**"; Revelation 13:11: Beast with lamb-like appearance but dragon's voice |
| **Wine** | Doctrines/Teachings | Jeremiah 51:7: "Babylon... made all the earth **drunk**" (false doctrine); Revelation 17:2: "wine of her fornication" |
| **Mark** | Sign of allegiance/loyalty | Revelation 13:16-17: Mark on forehead (belief) or hand (actions) |
| **Seal** | Sign of ownership/protection | Ezekiel 20:12, 20: Sabbath is God's **sign/seal**; Revelation 7:2-3 |
| **Forehead** | Mind/Belief/Conscious choice | Deuteronomy 6:6-8; 11:18: God's Word "as frontlets between your eyes" (in the mind); Revelation 13:16; 14:9: Mark received on forehead = intellectual acceptance/belief |
| **Hand** | Actions/Works/Compliance | Deuteronomy 6:8; 11:18: God's Word "as a sign on your hand" (in actions); Revelation 13:16; 14:9: Mark on hand = outward compliance in conduct/work regardless of belief |

#### **Why "Beasts from the Sea" Matters**

**Daniel 7:3**: "Four great beasts came up **from the sea**"

- **Sea** = Densely populated regions with political turmoil and warfare
- **Beast rising from sea** = Kingdom emerging from conquest and conflict among nations
- **Examples**: 
  - Babylon, Medo-Persia, Greece, Rome all arose through warfare in heavily populated regions
  - Conquered existing kingdoms and peoples
  - Emerged from the turbulent "sea" of Mediterranean/Middle Eastern civilization

**Revelation 13:11**: "Beast coming up **out of the earth**"

- **Earth/Land** = Sparsely populated, previously uninhabited territory
- **Beast rising from earth** = Kingdom emerging peacefully in relatively empty land
- **Example**: United States arose in sparsely populated North America, not through conquering densely populated empires

#### **Why Symbols Matter**

Understanding these biblical symbols is **not optional** - it's essential for correct interpretation:

1. **Prevents speculation** - We use Scripture to interpret Scripture, not human imagination
2. **Reveals prophetic identity** - Symbols identify specific powers with precision
3. **Shows fulfillment** - Historical events match symbolic descriptions exactly
4. **Confirms divine origin** - Only God could predict centuries in advance using symbolic language that history would fulfill

**Key Principle**: "No prophecy of Scripture is of any private interpretation" (2 Peter 1:20). The Bible interprets its own symbols - we must let Scripture define the meaning, not impose our own ideas.

---

### **Daniel's Two Visions of World Empires**

The Bible provides two parallel prophecies revealing the succession of world empires from Babylon to the end times:

#### **Daniel 2 - The Statue (Nebuchadnezzar's Dream)**

> "You, O king, were watching; and behold, a great image! This great image, whose splendor was excellent, stood before you; and its form was awesome. This image's head was of fine gold, its chest and arms of silver, its belly and thighs of bronze, its legs of iron, its feet partly of iron and partly of clay." (Daniel 2:31-33)

**Interpretation (Daniel 2:37-43)**:

**Daniel Identifies the First Kingdom**:
> "You, O king, are a king of kings. For the God of heaven has given you a kingdom, power, strength, and glory; and wherever the children of men dwell, or the beasts of the field and the birds of the heaven, He has given them into your hand, and has made you ruler over them all—**you are this head of gold**. But after you shall arise another kingdom inferior to yours; then another, a third kingdom of bronze, which shall rule over all the earth. And the fourth kingdom shall be as strong as iron." (Daniel 2:37-40)

**Biblical and Historical Succession**:

| **Part of Statue** | **Metal** | **Kingdom** | **Time Period** | **Biblical/Historical Evidence** |
|-------------------|----------|------------|----------------|--------------------------------|
| Head | Gold | **Babylon** | 605-539 BCE | **Daniel 2:37-38**: "You are this head of gold" (Nebuchadnezzar) |
| Chest/Arms | Silver | **Medo-Persia** | 539-331 BCE | **Daniel 5:28-31**: "Your kingdom has been divided, and given to the Medes and Persians... Darius the Mede received the kingdom" - Babylon conquered by Medo-Persia |
| Belly/Thighs | Bronze | **Greece** | 331-168 BCE | **Daniel 8:20-21**: "The ram... are the kings of Media and Persia. And the male goat is the kingdom of Greece" - History records Alexander the Great conquered Medo-Persia (331 BCE) |
| Legs | Iron | **Rome** | 168 BCE - 476 CE | **Daniel 2:40**: "The fourth kingdom shall be as strong as iron" - History records Rome conquered Greece (Battle of Pydna, 168 BCE) |
| Feet/Toes | **Iron & Clay** | **Divided Rome** | **476 CE - Present** | **Daniel 2:41-43**: "The kingdom shall be divided... they will mingle... but they will not adhere to one another" - Western Rome fell 476 CE, divided into European kingdoms that remain today |

**Key Point**: Daniel's prophecy has been 100% accurate through history. The first four kingdoms (Babylon, Medo-Persia, Greece, Rome) are confirmed by both Scripture and historical record. The fifth phase (Divided Rome) continues to the present day—exactly as prophesied.

#### **Daniel 7 - The Four Beasts**

> "Daniel spoke, saying, 'I saw in my vision by night, and behold, the four winds of heaven were stirring up the Great Sea. And four great beasts came up from the sea, each different from the other.'" (Daniel 7:2-3)

**The Four Beasts**:

| **Beast** | **Description** | **Kingdom** | **Time Period** |
|----------|----------------|------------|----------------|
| **Lion** with eagle's wings | Babylon's power and swiftness | Babylon | 605-539 BCE |
| **Bear** with three ribs | Medo-Persian conquests | Medo-Persia | 539-331 BCE |
| **Leopard** with 4 wings/heads | Greece's rapid expansion under Alexander | Greece | 331-168 BCE |
| **Terrifying Beast** with iron teeth, 10 horns | Rome's crushing power, divided kingdoms | Rome → Divided Europe | 168 BCE - Present |

**Biblical Evidence for Interpretation**:
> "These great beasts, which are four, are **four kings** which arise out of the earth... The fourth beast shall be **the fourth kingdom** on earth." (Daniel 7:17, 23)

**Gabriel the Angel Confirms the Same Kingdoms (Daniel 8)**:

In Daniel 8, the angel Gabriel explicitly identifies the kingdoms by name, confirming that Daniel's visions consistently describe the same prophetic sequence:

> **Daniel 8:20-21** - "The ram which you saw, having the two horns—they are **the kings of Media and Persia**. And the male goat is **the kingdom of Greece**. The great horn that is between its eyes is the first king."

**Key Point**: Gabriel directly names Medo-Persia and Greece as the second and third kingdoms. Combined with Daniel's identification of Babylon as the first (Daniel 2:37-38: "You are this head of gold"), and historical evidence of Rome conquering Greece, the prophetic sequence is unmistakable:
1. **Babylon** (named by Daniel in Daniel 2:38)
2. **Medo-Persia** (named by Gabriel in Daniel 8:20)
3. **Greece** (named by Gabriel in Daniel 8:21)
4. **Rome** (identified by description and historical succession)

This divine interpretation removes all speculation—God Himself, through His prophet Daniel and the angel Gabriel, identifies these world empires by name.

---

### **The Ten Horns: Division of the Roman Empire**

**Daniel 7:7-8**:
> "After this I saw in the night visions, and behold, a fourth beast, dreadful and terrible, exceedingly strong. It had huge iron teeth; it was devouring, breaking in pieces, and trampling the residue with its feet. It was different from all the beasts that were before it, and **it had ten horns**. I was considering the horns, and there was **another horn, a little one, coming up among them**, before whom **three of the first horns were plucked out by the roots**; and there, in this horn, were eyes like the eyes of a man, and a mouth speaking pompous words."

**Interpretation Daniel 7:24-25**:
> "The **ten horns are ten kings** who shall arise from this kingdom. And another shall rise after them; He shall be different from the first ones, and **shall subdue three kings**. He shall speak pompous words against the Most High, shall persecute the saints of the Most High, and shall intend to change times and law. Then the saints shall be given into his hand for a time and times and half a time." (Daniel 7:24-25)

#### **The Ten Kingdoms of Divided Rome (476 CE - 538 CE)**

After the fall of Western Rome in 476 CE, the empire fragmented into ten major tribal kingdoms:

| **Kingdom** | **Modern Location** | **Religion** | **Fate** |
|------------|---------------------|-------------|----------|
| 1. **Alemanni** | Germany/Switzerland | Catholic | Survived → Germany |
| 2. **Franks** | France | Catholic | Survived → France |
| 3. **Burgundians** | Switzerland/Eastern France | Catholic | Survived → Switzerland |
| 4. **Suevi** | Portugal/NW Spain | Catholic | Survived → Portugal |
| 5. **Visigoths** | Spain | Catholic (after 589 CE) | Survived → Spain |
| 6. **Anglo-Saxons** | England | Catholic (after 597 CE) | Survived → England |
| 7. **Heruli** | Italy | **Arian** | **Uprooted 493 CE** |
| 8. **Vandals** | North Africa | **Arian** | **Uprooted 534 CE** |
| 9. **Ostrogoths** | Italy | **Arian** | **Uprooted 538 CE** |
| 10. **Lombards** | Northern Italy | Catholic (after 7th century) | Survived → Italy |

#### **The Three Horns Uprooted by the Little Horn (Papal Rome)**

**Daniel 7:8**:
> "Before whom **three of the first horns were plucked out by the roots**."

**The Three Arian Kingdoms Eliminated**:

**1. Heruli (493 CE)**:
- **Location**: Italy (controlled Rome)
- **Religion**: Arian Christianity (rejected Trinity, papal authority)
- **Elimination**: Theodoric the Ostrogoth defeated Odoacer the Heruli king
- **Significance**: Removed Arian control of Rome

**2. Vandals (534 CE)**:
- **Location**: North Africa (Carthage)
- **Religion**: Arian Christianity
- **Persecution**: Actively persecuted Catholics in North Africa
- **Elimination**: Byzantine Emperor Justinian sent General Belisarius to destroy them
- **Significance**: Eliminated major Arian power opposing papal doctrine

**3. Ostrogoths (538 CE)**:
- **Location**: Italy (including Rome)
- **Religion**: Arian Christianity
- **Resistance**: Opposed papal supremacy in Rome
- **Elimination**: Byzantine forces under Belisarius finally defeated them in 538 CE
- **Significance**: **Final obstacle removed** - papal supremacy established in Rome
- **Prophetic Marker**: **538 CE begins the 1,260-year papal dominance** (538-1798 CE)

#### **Why These Three Were Uprooted**

**Theological Opposition**:
- All three were **Arian Christians** (believed Christ was created, not eternally God)
- Rejected papal authority and Trinitarian doctrine
- Posed theological threat to Roman Catholic Church

**Geographic Threat**:
- **Heruli and Ostrogoths controlled Italy/Rome** - direct obstacle to papal political power
- **Vandals controlled North Africa** - major Arian power base threatening Catholic unity

**Political Necessity**:
- For papacy to establish supremacy, these kingdoms had to be eliminated
- Byzantine Emperor Justinian (Catholic) supported papal authority
- Issued decree in 533 CE recognizing Pope as "head of all churches"
- Used military force to remove Arian kingdoms blocking papal supremacy

#### **The Seven Surviving Kingdoms**

After the three Arian kingdoms were uprooted, seven Catholic kingdoms remained and evolved into modern European nations:

| **Ancient Kingdom** | **Modern Nation** |
|-------------------|------------------|
| **Alemanni** | Germany |
| **Franks** | France |
| **Burgundians** | Switzerland |
| **Suevi** | Portugal |
| **Visigoths** | Spain |
| **Anglo-Saxons** | England (United Kingdom) |
| **Lombards** | Italy |

These nations became the foundation of **Catholic Europe** - accepting papal authority and forming the "iron-clay mixture" where the papacy (iron) mingles with but doesn't fully control European nations (clay).

**Daniel 7:25** - The 1,260-Year Prophecy:
> "And he shall speak great words against the most High, and shall wear out the saints of the most High, and think to change times and laws: and they shall be given into his hand until **a time and times and half a time**. 
- **Time** = 1 prophetic year = 360 days
- **Times** = 2 prophetic years = 720 days
- **Half a time** = ½ prophetic year = 180 days
- **Total** = 3.5 prophetic years = **1,260 prophetic days**

#### **Connection to the Ten Toes (Daniel 2)**

The **ten horns** of Daniel 7 correspond to the **ten toes** (iron mixed with clay) of Daniel 2:
- **Ten toes** = Ten kingdoms of divided Rome

- **Clay element** = Secular European nations
- **Mixed but not adhering** = Church-state relationship (influence without full control)

**Why Iron Represents Both Imperial and Papal Rome**:
- **Daniel 2:40**: "The fourth kingdom shall be as strong as iron"
- **Continuity**: The iron (Rome) doesn't disappear - it continues in the feet/toes mixed with clay
- **Evolution**: Imperial Rome (legs) → Papal Rome (feet/toes) - same kingdom, different phase
- **Geographic**: Both headquartered in Rome - Vatican occupies the same city as the ancient Roman Empire
- **Authority Structure**: Vatican preserved Roman organizational hierarchy, legal system, titles, and Latin language
- **Prophetic Identification**: The "little horn" (Daniel 7:8, 24-25) arose from among the ten kingdoms of divided Rome - it's part of the fourth beast, not a separate fifth kingdom
- **Unique Fulfillment**: Vatican/Papacy is the ONLY entity in world history that originates from Rome AND functions as both a political state (Vatican City) and religious authority (Catholic Church) - no other nation or institution fits this dual political-religious identity emerging from the fourth beast

**Modern Fulfillment**:
- The same seven nations (plus others formed later) still exist in Europe
- Vatican still maintains diplomatic relations and influence

- Nations maintain sovereignty but Vatican exerts religious-political pressure as moral arbiter
- Project 2025 in USA shows same pattern: religious authority seeking to influence secular government through moral and spiritual leadership claims

### **Revelation Expands Daniel's Prophecy**

**Daniel and Revelation describe the same power from different perspectives**. Daniel gives the historical framework; Revelation adds spiritual warfare details and end-time fulfillment. Together they form a complete prophetic picture.

#### **The Beast from the Sea (Revelation 13:1-10) - The Papacy**

**Revelation 13:1-2**:
> "Then I stood on the sand of the sea. And I saw a **beast rising up out of the sea**, having seven heads and ten horns, and on his horns ten crowns, and on his heads a blasphemous name. Now the beast which I saw was like a leopard, his feet were like the feet of a bear, and his mouth like the mouth of a lion. **The dragon gave him his power, his throne, and great authority**."

**Identifying Marks of the First Beast**:

| **Prophetic Characteristic** | **Biblical Reference** | **Historical Fulfillment** |
|----------------------------|----------------------|---------------------------|
| **Rises from the sea** (densely populated area) | Revelation 13:1 | Papal Rome arose from populated Mediterranean/European region |
| **Seven heads** (seven mountains/kings) | Revelation 13:1; 17:9 | Located in Rome, city on seven hills; seven forms of Roman government |
| **Ten horns** (ten kingdoms) | Revelation 13:1; 17:12 | Ten kingdoms of divided Western Roman Empire (476 CE) |

| **Like leopard, bear, lion** | Revelation 13:2 | Combines characteristics of Daniel's beasts (Babylon, Medo-Persia, Greece) - papal system incorporated pagan doctrines from all three empires into Christianity |
| **Dragon gave power** | Revelation 13:2 | Satan working through pagan Rome transferred power to papal Rome |
| **Authority 42 months** (1,260 days) | Revelation 13:5 | Papal supremacy 1,260 years (538-1798 CE) using day-year principle |
| **Speaks blasphemies against God** | Revelation 13:5-6 | Claims divine titles, papal infallibility, authority over God's law |
| **Makes war with saints** | Revelation 13:7 | Inquisitions, persecution, martyrdom of all who held biblical truth over church tradition - Bible translators, Scripture distributors, those who rejected papal authority, Sabbath-keepers, and anyone exposing papal errors (1,260 years) |
| **Authority over all tribes/tongues** | Revelation 13:7 | Vatican claims universal jurisdiction over all Christians worldwide |
| **Deadly wound** | Revelation 13:3 | Pope imprisoned by Napoleon (1798 CE), papal temporal power ended |
| **Wound healed** | Revelation 13:3 | Vatican City restored as sovereign state (1929 Lateran Treaty) |
| **All the world wondered** | Revelation 13:3 | Modern global influence, diplomatic relations with 180+ nations |

**Connection to Daniel's Little Horn**:

| **Daniel 7** | **Revelation 13** | **Same Power** |
|-------------|------------------|----------------|
| Little horn among ten kingdoms (Daniel 7:8, 24) | Beast from the sea with ten horns (Revelation 13:1-2) | Papal Rome arising from divided Roman Empire |

| Three horns uprooted (Daniel 7:8, 24) | Receives authority after defeating obstacles | Three Arian kingdoms eliminated (493-538 CE) |

**The 1,260-Year Prophecy Repeated**:

Scripture gives the same time period in **four different ways** to emphasize its importance:
- **Daniel 7:25**: "a time and times and the dividing of time" (3.5 prophetic years = 1,260 days = 1,260 literal years)
- **Revelation 12:6**: "one thousand two hundred and sixty days"
- **Revelation 12:14**: "a time and times and half a time"
- **Revelation 13:5**: "forty-two months" (42 months × 30 days = 1,260 days)

**Day-Year Principle** (Ezekiel 4:6; Numbers 14:34): One prophetic day = one literal year
**Result**: 1,260 prophetic days = **1,260 literal years** (538-1798 CE)

**Why the Beast Combines Leopard, Bear, and Lion Characteristics**:

**Revelation 13:2** describes a unique characteristic of the first beast (papal Rome):
> "Now the beast which I saw was **like a leopard, his feet were like the feet of a bear, and his mouth like the mouth of a lion**."

This is prophetically significant. In **Daniel 7**, each beast represented a separate kingdom:
- **Lion** = Babylon (Daniel 7:4)
- **Bear** = Medo-Persia (Daniel 7:5)
- **Leopard** = Greece (Daniel 7:6)
- **Fourth Beast** = Rome (Daniel 7:7)

But Revelation's beast **combines all three previous beasts** into one. This reveals something profound about the papal system: it didn't just succeed Rome politically—it **absorbed and incorporated the pagan religious systems** of all three previous empires into a Christianized form.

**Historical Fulfillment - Pagan Doctrines Absorbed**:

**From Babylon**:
- **Sun worship** → Sunday sacredness (Sol Invictus became "the Lord's Day")
- **Mystery religion elements** → Secret rites, confessional system, priestly mediation
- **Priestly hierarchy** → Pontifex Maximus (Babylonian high priest title adopted by Pope)
- **Queen of Heaven worship** → Transformed into Mary veneration

**The Baal-to-Sunday Connection - Ancient Sun Worship Continued**:

Baal worship is linked to Sunday primarily through the **historical identification of Baal as a sun-god worshipped on the first day of the week**, often contrasted with the biblical **seventh-day Sabbath**. This connection reveals the deep pagan roots of Sunday observance.

**"Baal" Means "Lord" - Sunday Called "The Lord's Day"**:

The most striking connection between Baal worship and Sunday observance is **linguistic and theological**:

**The Name "Baal" Literally Means "Lord"**:
- **Hebrew**: בַּעַל (*Ba'al*) = "Lord," "Master," "Owner," "Husband"
- **Usage**: Title of authority and deity worship
- **Biblical Context**: When Israelites worshiped Baal, they were calling the sun god "Lord"

**Sunday Is Called "The Lord's Day"**:
- **Catholic terminology**: "Dies Domini" (Latin) = "Day of the Lord"
- **Romance languages** preserve this title:
  - Spanish: **Domingo** = "Lord's Day"
  - Italian: **Domenica** = "Lord's Day"
  - Portuguese: **Domingo** = "Lord's Day"
  - French: **Dimanche** (from Latin *Dominica*) = "Lord's Day"

**The Damning Connection**:

1. **Ancient Israel**: Worshiped the sun god on the first day, calling him **"Baal" (Lord)**
2. **Modern Christianity**: Worships on the first day, calling it **"the Lord's Day"**
3. **Same practice, same title, different language**—but the **same demonic entity**

**Biblical Condemnation of Calling Baal "Lord"**:

God explicitly condemned Israel for calling Baal "Lord":

**Hosea 2:16-17**:
> "And it shall be, in that day," says the LORD, "that you will call Me 'My Husband,' and **no longer call Me 'My Master' (Baali)**. For I will take from her mouth the names of the Baals, and they shall be remembered by their name no more."

**Hebrew Insight**:
- "My Husband" = *Ishi* (intimate relationship term)
- "My Master" = *Baali* (using the name/title of the false god)
- God is saying: **Stop using Baal's title ("Lord") to address Me**

**The Prophetic Irony**:

God told Israel through Hosea: **"Stop calling Me 'Baali' (Lord in the Baal sense)"**—yet modern Christianity observes **"the Lord's Day" (Baal's sun worship day)** and claims it honors Christ.

**Which "Lord"?**

When Sunday is called "the Lord's Day," a critical question arises: **Which lord?**

1. **Jesus Christ**, who said "the Son of Man is Lord of the **Sabbath**" (Mark 2:28)—the seventh day (Saturday)?
2. **Or Baal**, the ancient sun god whose worship day (Sunday/first day) was Christianized and given the title "Lord's Day"?

**The Historical Reality**:
- **Jesus never called Sunday "the Lord's Day"**
- **Jesus explicitly claimed to be Lord of the Sabbath** (Saturday)—Mark 2:28
- **Sunday worship came from Constantine's sun worship**, not from Christ
- **"The Lord's Day" title for Sunday** perpetuates Baal's name ("Lord") for Baal's worship day (sun-day)

**"The Lord's Day" in Revelation 1:10**:

Many claim **Revelation 1:10** ("I was in the Spirit on the Lord's Day") refers to Sunday. But context proves otherwise:

**Mark 2:28** - Jesus declares:
> "Therefore the Son of Man is **Lord even of the Sabbath**."

- Jesus explicitly identifies **the Sabbath** as His day
- If any day is "the Lord's Day," it's the **Sabbath** (seventh day)
- The phrase "Lord's Day" in Revelation 1:10 most naturally refers to the day **Jesus called His own**—the Sabbath

**Sunday was never called "the Lord's Day" in apostolic times**—that title came later, when the church had already compromised with Constantine's sun worship.

**The Title Transfer**:

The trajectory is clear:
1. **Ancient**: "Baal" (Lord) worshiped on sun-day (first day of the week)
2. **Constantine Era**: Sun worship merged with Christianity; Sunday becomes "sacred"
3. **Medieval Catholic Church**: Sunday officially titled "the Lord's Day" (*Dies Domini*)
4. **Modern**: Entire Christian world calls Sunday "the Lord's Day"—**using Baal's title for Baal's worship day**

**God's Perspective**:

Just as God told Israel through Hosea, **"Stop calling Me 'Baali' (My Lord/Master)"** because they were using the false god's name, so today God says:

**Stop calling Sunday "the Lord's Day"**—it is **Baal's day**, rebranded with Christian terminology, but still the **same pagan sun worship** that carried the death penalty under Mosaic law.

**The Title Belongs to the Sabbath**:

If any day deserves the title "the Lord's Day," it is the **seventh-day Sabbath**, because:
- **God blessed it** (Genesis 2:3)
- **God sanctified it** (Genesis 2:3)
- **God commanded it** (Exodus 20:8-11)
- **Jesus claimed Lordship over it** (Mark 2:28)
- **Jesus observed it** (Luke 4:16)
- **Apostles observed it** (Acts 13:14, 16:13, 17:2, 18:4)

**Calling Sunday "the Lord's Day" while ignoring the biblical Sabbath is spiritual adultery**—honoring Baal under the pretense of honoring Christ.

**Prominent Sun Deities Across Ancient Cultures**:

Throughout ancient history, sun worship was universal, with different cultures naming their sun gods:
- **Baal** (Canaanite/Phoenician) - "Lord" or "Master," supreme fertility and sun deity
- **Moloch** (Canaanite/Ammonite) - **Same entity as Baal**, also called Molech, Milcom; demanded child sacrifice through fire
- **Shamash** (Mesopotamian/Babylonian) - Sun god and judge
- **Ra and Aten** (Egyptian) - Solar deities ruling over creation
- **Apollo/Helios** (Greco-Roman) - God of the sun, light, and prophecy
- **Sol Invictus** (Roman) - "Unconquered Sun," official cult of late Roman Empire
- **Mithra** (Persian/Roman Mystery Cult) - Sun god in mystery religion popular among Roman soldiers
- **Surya** (Hindu) - Solar deity
- **Ashtoreth/Astarte** (Canaanite) - Associated with Venus/morning star, but part of Baal cult system

**Baal and Moloch - The Same Demonic Entity**:

**Baal** and **Moloch** (also spelled Molech or Milcom) are **the same entity** with different regional names and emphases. Both represent the Canaanite sun god system that demanded the most horrific form of worship: **child sacrifice**.

**Biblical Evidence They Are the Same**:

**1. Same Geographic Region and Worship System**:
- Both worshiped in Canaan, Phoenicia, Ammon
- Both part of the same pagan pantheon opposing Israel
- Both demanded fire sacrifice
- Both condemned together in Scripture as the same abomination

**2. Interchangeable References**:

**Jeremiah 32:35** connects Baal directly to child sacrifice:
> "And they built the high places of **Baal** which are in the Valley of the Son of Hinnom, to **cause their sons and their daughters to pass through the fire to Molech**, which I did not command them, nor did it come into My mind that they should do this abomination, to cause Judah to sin."

Notice: Built high places to **Baal**, but sacrificed to **Molech**—the same location, same practice, showing they are the same entity.

**3. Same Worship Practice - Child Sacrifice Through Fire**:

**Leviticus 18:21**:
> "And you shall not let any of your descendants **pass through the fire to Molech**, nor shall you profane the name of your God: I am the LORD."

**Leviticus 20:2-5**:
> "Again, you shall say to the children of Israel: 'Whoever of the children of Israel, or of the strangers who dwell in Israel, who gives any of his descendants to **Molech**, he shall surely be put to death. The people of the land shall stone him with stones... Then I will set My face against that man and against his family; and I will cut him off from his people, and all who prostitute themselves with him to **commit harlotry with Molech**.'"

**2 Kings 23:10** - King Josiah's reforms destroyed Molech worship sites:
> "And he defiled Topheth, which is in the Valley of the Son of Hinnom, that no man might make his son or his daughter **pass through the fire to Molech**."

**The Horrific Practice**:
- **Bronze statue** of Moloch/Baal heated until red-hot
- **Living infants placed in the statue's arms** or thrown into fire pit
- **Drums and music** played loudly to drown out children's screams
- Parents believed this sacrifice would bring prosperity, good crops, military victory
- Practiced in **Valley of Hinnom** (Gehenna) outside Jerusalem

**4. Same Condemnation - God's Extreme Judgment**:

God's response to Baal/Moloch worship was **the most severe judgment** in Scripture:

**Jeremiah 19:4-6**:
> "Because they have forsaken Me and made this an alien place, because they have burned incense in it to other gods whom neither they, their fathers, nor the kings of Judah have known, and have **filled this place with the blood of the innocents** (they have also built the high places of Baal, to **burn their sons with fire for burnt offerings to Baal**, which I did not command or speak, nor did it come into My mind), therefore behold, the days are coming... that this place shall no more be called Tophet or the Valley of the Son of Hinnom, but the **Valley of Slaughter**."

**Jeremiah 7:31**:
> "And they have built the high places of Tophet, which is in the Valley of the Son of Hinnom, to **burn their sons and their daughters in the fire**, which I did not command, nor did it come into My heart."

**God declares this practice "did not come into My heart"** - so abhorrent that even God's infinite mind never conceived such evil. This reveals the **demonic depravity** of Baal/Moloch worship.

**5. Death Penalty Commanded**:

**Leviticus 20:2**:
> "Whoever of the children of Israel, or of the strangers who dwell in Israel, who gives any of his descendants to Molech, **he shall surely be put to death**. The people of the land shall **stone him with stones**."

This is the same penalty prescribed for:
- Sun worship (Deuteronomy 17:2-5)
- Idolatry (Deuteronomy 13:6-10)
- Sabbath-breaking (Numbers 15:32-36)

**Why?** Because Baal/Moloch worship was the **ultimate abomination**—combining false worship, sun worship, and murder of innocent children.

**The Connection to Sunday Worship**:

The same demonic entity (Baal/Moloch) that demanded:
- **Sun worship** on the first day of the week
- **Child sacrifice** as the ultimate offering
- **Fire rituals** as worship practice

Has had its **sun worship day** (Sunday) **Christianized and made mandatory** under the label "the Lord's Day."

**Modern Parallel - Abortion as Child Sacrifice**:

The spirit of Moloch/Baal continues today:
- **Ancient practice**: Sacrificing children to false god for prosperity, convenience, personal benefit
- **Modern practice**: Abortion—ending children's lives for financial reasons, convenience, personal choice
- **Same demonic influence**: Different method, same result—innocent blood shed
- **Same justifications**: "My body, my choice" / "Economic necessity" / "Not the right time"

**Baal/Moloch worship has never ceased**—it has merely **changed form**.

**The Prophetic Warning**:

The same system that:
- Instituted **sun worship** (Baal) as sacred Christian tradition (Sunday)
- Demanded **child sacrifice** (Moloch) in ancient times

Will enforce **Sunday worship** globally and ultimately demand **death** for those who refuse (Revelation 13:15). The leopard's spots remain—the same demonic power operating under Christian terminology.

**God's judgment on those who sacrificed children to Baal/Moloch was severe**. How much more severe will be the judgment on those who enforce the worship day of this same entity while calling it "Christian tradition"?

**The Syncretism Process - How Sun Gods Merged**:

These sun deities were not the "same entity" with different names, but underwent a **syncretic process** in the late Roman Empire:
1. **Baal** (Canaanite) influenced Phoenician and Mediterranean cultures
2. **Apollo/Helios** (Greek) became the dominant Greco-Roman sun god
3. **Sol Invictus** (Roman) was declared supreme sun god by Emperor Aurelian (270-275 CE)
4. **Mithras** (Persian mystery cult) merged with Sol Invictus in Roman military circles
5. All converged into the Roman cult of **Sol Invictus** ("Unconquered Sun") as part of the "one god, one empire" ideology

This was the **religious atmosphere when Constantine "converted"** to Christianity in 312 CE. Constantine himself was a **lifelong sun-worshipper** who:
- Kept the title **Pontifex Maximus** (High Priest of sun worship)
- Minted coins with **Sol Invictus** until 320 CE (8 years after "conversion")
- Made **Sunday a civil rest day** in 321 CE, explicitly calling it "the venerable day of the Sun"
- Never abandoned sun worship imagery in his political symbolism

**Biblical Warnings Against Sun Worship**:

God repeatedly warned Israel against adopting sun worship from surrounding pagan nations:

**Deuteronomy 4:19**:
> "And take heed, lest you lift your eyes to heaven, and when you see the sun, the moon, and the stars, all the host of heaven, **you feel driven to worship them and serve them**, which the LORD your God has given to all the peoples under the whole heaven as a heritage."

**Deuteronomy 17:2-5** prescribes the **death penalty** for sun worship:
> "If there is found among you... a man or a woman who... **has gone and served other gods and worshiped them, either the sun or moon** or any of the host of heaven, which I have not commanded... then you shall bring out to your gates that man or woman who has committed that wicked thing, and **shall stone to death** that man or woman with stones."

**2 Kings 23:5, 11** - King Josiah's reforms removed sun worship from Israel:
> "Then he removed the idolatrous priests... those who **burned incense to the sun**, to the moon, to the constellations, and to all the host of heaven... He removed the **horses that the kings of Judah had dedicated to the sun** at the entrance to the house of the LORD."

**Ezekiel 8:16-18** - God shows Ezekiel the abomination of sun worship:
> "So He brought me into the inner court of the LORD's house; and there, at the door of the temple of the LORD, between the porch and the altar, were about **twenty-five men with their backs toward the temple of the LORD and their faces toward the east, and they were worshiping the sun toward the east**. And He said to me, 'Have you seen this, O son of man? Is it a trivial thing to the house of Judah to commit the abominations which they commit here?'"

**This Ancient Abomination Continues in Church Architecture Today**:

The practice God condemned in Ezekiel 8:16-18 has been **institutionalized in Catholic and Protestant church architecture** through the tradition of **"eastward orientation"** (also called "liturgical east"):

**The Architectural Tradition**:
- **Catholic churches** are traditionally built with the altar at the **east end**
- **Protestant churches** often follow the same eastward-facing design
- The priest/minister stands **behind the altar facing east** during services
- The congregation sits **facing east** toward the altar
- Official justification: Facing the direction of Christ's return, Jerusalem, or the rising sun as symbol of resurrection

**The Damning Reality - Backs to God, Faces to the Sun**:

This is **exactly what God called an abomination** in Ezekiel's vision:
- **Ezekiel 8:16**: "With their **backs toward the temple of the LORD** and their **faces toward the east**"
- **Modern practice**: Congregation has backs to the west (where they entered), faces toward the east (where altar stands)
- **Result**: During worship services, prayers, and ceremonies, the assembly is **literally facing east—the direction of the rising sun**

**Historical Adoption from Pagan Sun Worship**:

This was not a biblical practice but a **pagan tradition absorbed into Christianity**:

1. **Pagan temples** (Greek, Roman, Egyptian) faced east toward the rising sun
2. **Sol Invictus temples** in Rome faced east for sun worship
3. **Early church buildings** initially had no fixed orientation
4. **After Constantine** (4th century), eastward orientation became standard church practice
5. **By medieval period**, it was mandatory Catholic architectural requirement
6. **Protestant Reformation** largely retained this Catholic architectural tradition despite rejecting other Catholic practices

**Catholic and Orthodox Teaching on Eastward Orientation**:

The Catholic Church explicitly teaches eastward orientation:
- **Catechism references** to facing east during prayer
- **Liturgical tradition**: Priest faces east (ad orientem) during Mass
- **Symbolism claimed**: Christ as "Sun of Righteousness," resurrection, Second Coming from the east
- **Modern practice**: Vatican II allowed priest to face congregation (versus populum), but traditional Latin Mass retains eastward facing

**The Prophetic Parallel**:

| **Ezekiel's Vision (Ancient Israel)** | **Modern Church Practice** |
|--------------------------------------|---------------------------|
| 25 men in temple court | Congregation in church building |
| Backs toward the temple of the LORD | Backs toward west entrance |
| Faces toward the east | Faces toward east altar |
| Worshiping the sun toward the east | Worship service facing east |
| God calls it an **abomination** | Churches call it **sacred tradition** |
| Between porch and altar | Between nave and sanctuary/altar |

**God's Response in Ezekiel's Day**:

God's reaction to this practice was **severe**:

**Ezekiel 8:17-18**:
> "Then He said to me, 'Have you seen this, O son of man? Is it a trivial thing to the house of Judah to commit the abominations which they commit here? For they have filled the land with violence; then they have returned to provoke Me to anger. Indeed they put the branch to their nose. **Therefore I also will act in fury. My eye will not spare nor will I have pity; and though they cry in My ears with a loud voice, I will not hear them**.'"

The practice was so offensive to God that He declared He would **not hear their prayers** despite loud crying. This is the same practice now considered **sacred Christian tradition**.

**The Sun Worship Connection Remains**:

Despite claims that eastward orientation symbolizes Christ's return or resurrection, the historical origin is unmistakable:
- **Timing**: Adopted after Constantine merged Christianity with sun worship
- **Direction**: East—direction of the rising sun (Sol Invictus, Apollo, Ra, Baal)
- **Pattern**: Mirrors pagan temple architecture, not biblical tabernacle/temple design
- **Result**: Continuation of the sun worship practice God condemned as abomination

**Biblical Temple Orientation Was Different**:

God's original design had **no eastward sun worship orientation**:
- **Tabernacle entrance**: Faced **east**, requiring Israelites to face **west** (toward Holy of Holies) during worship—**away from the rising sun**
- **Solomon's Temple**: Same design—entrance east, Holy of Holies west
- **Worshipers faced west** toward God's presence, **not east** toward the sun
- **Deliberate design**: God ensured His people would **not worship facing the sun's rising**

**The Abomination Persists**:

What God called an abomination in Ezekiel 8:16-18 has been:
- **Adopted as Christian tradition**
- **Codified in church architecture**
- **Practiced for over 1,600 years**
- **Defended as symbolizing Christ** (while maintaining pagan sun worship orientation)
- **Retained even by Protestant reformers** who rejected other Catholic traditions

This is another example of **Babylon's wine**—a pagan practice absorbed into Christianity, given Christian symbolism and terminology, and enforced as sacred tradition. The leopard's spots remain unchanged.

**King Jeroboam's Counterfeit Worship System**:

After Solomon's kingdom divided, King Jeroboam established a **counterfeit worship system** to prevent Israel from returning to Jerusalem:

**1 Kings 12:28-33** records he:
- Made **two golden calves** (representing Baal/sun god)
- Declared **"Here are your gods, O Israel, which brought you up from the land of Egypt"**
- Established worship at **Dan and Bethel** (instead of Jerusalem)
- Appointed **non-Levitical priests**
- Changed **feast times** ("devised in his own heart")

This pattern—**changing God's appointed worship day and system to something more convenient**—is exactly what papal Rome did with the Sabbath-to-Sunday change.

**From Baal Worship to Sunday Sacredness**:

The transition follows this historical progression:
1. **Old Testament Era**: Israel repeatedly warned against sun worship (Baal, Ashtoreth)
2. **Intertestamental Period**: Greek sun worship (Apollo/Helios) spreads through conquered territories
3. **Roman Empire**: Sol Invictus becomes official state cult (270s CE)
4. **Constantine Era**: Sunday worship merged with Christianity under Christian terminology (321 CE)
5. **Papal Rome**: Sunday declared sacred "Lord's Day," eventually enforced by church authority and civil law
6. **Modern Era**: Sunday laws enforced globally under environmental, labor, and religious justifications

**Result**: The same **sun worship God condemned in the Old Testament**—which carried the death penalty under Mosaic law—has been **Christianized and made mandatory** under the label "the Lord's Day." This is the wine of Babylon: pagan practice given a Christian name.

**From Medo-Persia**:
- **Religious-political authority fusion** → Church-state union (kings ruling as religious authorities)
- **Imperial decree enforcement** → Papal bulls and edicts enforced by civil governments
- **Hierarchical bureaucracy** → Administrative structure controlling vast territories

**From Greece**:
- **Immortal soul doctrine** → Borrowed from Greek philosophy (Plato), not Scripture
- **Eternal torment in hell** → Greek mythology (Hades, Tartarus) Christianized
- **Philosophical approach to theology** → Greek philosophy mixed with biblical teaching
- **Mystery schools** → Transformed into ecclesiastical education system

**Why This Matters**:

The beast's combined characteristics reveal that **papal Rome is not merely a political successor to the Roman Empire**—it is a **religious syncretism** that blended:
- Babylonian mystery religion
- Persian religious-political authority
- Greek philosophical concepts
- Roman governmental structure
- Biblical terminology and symbolism

**Result**: A system that **appears Christian** (uses Christian language, claims Christ's authority) but is built on a foundation of **pagan doctrines from all three previous empires**. This is why it's described as having characteristics of all three beasts—the pagan elements weren't discarded when Rome became "Christian" under Constantine; they were **absorbed, renamed, and Christianized**.

**Connection to the Sabbath Change**:

The Sabbath-to-Sunday change perfectly illustrates this pattern:
- **God's Command**: Seventh-day Sabbath (Exodus 20:8-11) - established at Creation
- **Pagan Practice**: Sun worship on Sunday (day of the sun god)
- **Papal Syncretism**: Changed biblical Sabbath to pagan Sunday, calling it "the Lord's Day"
- **Result**: Pagan practice given Christian label and enforced as divine command

This is the **wine of Babylon** (Revelation 17:2) - false doctrines that mix pagan traditions with Christianity, making nations spiritually drunk and unable to distinguish biblical truth from human tradition.

**Can the Leopard Change Its Spots? - Jeremiah 13:23 Applied to Papal Rome**

**Jeremiah 13:23** provides a sobering commentary on the nature of Revelation's leopard-like beast:
> "**Can the Ethiopian change his skin or the leopard its spots? Then may you also do good who are accustomed to do evil.**"

**Context of Jeremiah's Prophecy**:

God was speaking to Judah about their deeply ingrained wickedness. The question is **rhetorical**—the answer is obviously **no**. An Ethiopian cannot change his skin color; a leopard cannot change its spots. Likewise, those who are **"accustomed to do evil"** (literally "taught/trained to do evil") **cannot reform themselves** to do good. The Hebrew emphasizes habitual, learned behavior that has become second nature.

**Application to Revelation 13:2's Leopard-Like Beast**:

Revelation describes the papal system as **"like a leopard"** (Revelation 13:2). This is not accidental imagery—it connects directly to Jeremiah 13:23's metaphor:

1. **The Leopard's Spots Represent Papal Rome's Inherent Nature**:
   - The "spots" are the **pagan doctrines absorbed** from Babylon, Medo-Persia, and Greece
   - The system is **fundamentally built on paganism Christianized**
   - Like a leopard cannot remove its spots, **papal Rome cannot abandon its pagan foundation** without ceasing to exist

2. **"Accustomed to Do Evil" - 1,260 Years of Persecution**:
   - Daniel 7:25 and Revelation 13:7 prophesy the beast would **"make war with the saints"**
   - Historical fulfillment: **Inquisitions, martyrdom, persecution** (538-1798 CE)
   - Not isolated incidents but **systematic, institutionalized persecution** spanning over a millennium
   - The system was **"trained" and "accustomed"** to use force, coercion, and violence to maintain power

3. **Modern Claims of Reform Ring Hollow**:
   - Papal Rome has issued **apologies for past atrocities** (Crusades, Inquisitions, treatment of Jews, Indigenous peoples, etc.)
   - But the **fundamental doctrines remain unchanged**: papal supremacy, Sunday sacredness, tradition over Scripture, priestly mediation, etc.
   - The leopard still has its spots—**the pagan foundation persists under Christian terminology**
   - Jeremiah's question implies: Can you expect genuine reform from a system fundamentally "accustomed to do evil"?

4. **The Leopard's Prophetic Significance**:
   - **Leopard = Greece** in Daniel 7:6 (representing Greek philosophical influence)
   - Papal Rome incorporated **Greek philosophy** (immortal soul, eternal hell, Platonic thought) into theology
   - The leopard imagery shows this is **intrinsic to the system**, not a superficial adoption
   - Like spots define a leopard, **pagan philosophy defines papal theology**

5. **Cannot Change Without Ceasing to Be Itself**:
   - If papal Rome abandoned Sunday for Sabbath, it would invalidate 1,700+ years of tradition
   - If it rejected papal authority, it would cease to be "papal" Rome
   - If it removed all pagan doctrines, nothing distinctively "Catholic" would remain
   - **The system is incapable of biblical reform** because reform would mean self-destruction
   - This is precisely Jeremiah 13:23's point: Those accustomed to evil **cannot do good** without fundamental transformation

6. **Revelation 13:3's Wound "Healed" - The Leopard Returns**:
   - Deadly wound (1798) appeared to end papal power
   - Wound "healed" (1929 Lateran Treaty restored Vatican sovereignty)
   - Prophecy declares **"all the world wondered after the beast"** (Revelation 13:3)
   - The leopard didn't change its spots during the wound—it **returned with the same nature**
   - Modern Vatican diplomacy, ecumenism, and Sunday enforcement agenda prove **the spots remain**

**The Devil's Work Through a Christian Mirage**:

Papal Rome presents itself as the guardian of Christian truth, moral authority, and spiritual legitimacy. But Jeremiah 13:23 reveals the sobering reality: **a system fundamentally "accustomed to do evil" cannot genuinely reform**. The leopard-like beast of Revelation 13:2 is not merely *compared* to a leopard—it **is** a leopard in nature, unable to change its defining characteristics.

This is why Revelation describes it as the **wine of Babylon** (Revelation 17:2, 4; 18:3): It appears as wine (desirable, refined, Christian), but it is **spiritual poison** (pagan doctrines mixed with biblical terminology) that makes nations **drunk** (unable to discern truth from error).

**The Prophetic Warning**:

God's people are called to **"Come out of her, my people"** (Revelation 18:4). Why? Because the system **cannot change**. The leopard will not voluntarily remove its spots. The beast that was "accustomed to do evil" for 1,260 years will not suddenly become righteous. The wound healed, but **the nature remained the same**.

**The question is not whether papal Rome will reform—Jeremiah 13:23 declares it cannot. The question is whether God's people will recognize the leopard's spots and separate from its influence before the final crisis.**

#### **The Beast from the Earth (Revelation 13:11-18) - The United States**

**Revelation 13:11**:
> "Then I saw **another beast coming up out of the earth**, and he had **two horns like a lamb** and **spoke like a dragon**."

**Contrast Between the Two Beasts**:

| **First Beast (Papacy)** | **Second Beast (USA)** |
|-------------------------|----------------------|
| Rises from **sea** (densely populated) | Rises from **earth** (sparsely populated) |
| Has **ten horns** (kingdoms/powers) | Has **two horns** (two principles) |
| Like **leopard, bear, lion** (predatory) | Like a **lamb** (gentle, Christian) |
| **Openly blasphemous** from the start | **Appears righteous** but speaks like dragon |
| **Catholic/church power** | **Protestant/civil power** cooperating with churches |
| Medieval church-state **union** | Modern church-state **alliance** forming |
| First beast **receives** dragon's power | Second beast **exercises** first beast's authority |

**Identifying the Second Beast - United States**:

**Historical Timeline: 1798 - A Prophetic Transition Year**

**First Beast (Papacy) Receives Deadly Wound - 1798**:
- **February 1798**: French General Berthier (under Napoleon) entered Rome
- **Pope Pius VI imprisoned**, removed from Vatican
- Taken to France where he died in captivity (August 1799)
- **Papal temporal power ended** - completing the 1,260-year prophecy (538-1798 CE)
- This is the "deadly wound" referenced in Revelation 13:3

**Second Beast (United States) Rising - 1776-1798**:
- **July 4, 1776**: Declaration of Independence
- **1783**: Treaty of Paris - Britain recognizes U.S. independence
- **1787**: U.S. Constitution drafted
- **1789**: George Washington inaugurated as first president
- **1791**: Bill of Rights ratified (including religious freedom - First Amendment)
- **By 1798**: United States established as independent nation with constitutional government

**Why the United States Fits the Lamb-Like Beast Prophecy**:

**1. Timing - Rose When First Beast Wounded (1798)**:
- **Revelation 13:10-11**: "He who leads into captivity shall go into captivity... Here is the patience... of the saints. **Then I saw another beast**"
- First beast wounded: February 1798 (Pope imprisoned)
- Second beast rising: United States established 1776-1798 (Constitution, Bill of Rights, Washington presidency)
- **Prophetic transition**: Old World oppressor falls, New World refuge rises
- **1798 marked divine transition**: Papacy's 1,260-year persecution ended; United States offered haven from religious tyranny

**2. Geography - "Out of the Earth" (Sparsely Populated)**:
- **Revelation 13:11**: "Coming up out of the earth"
- **Earth** (Greek: *gē*) = Land, contrasting with turbulent "sea" (densely populated nations)
- United States arose in **sparsely populated North America**, not from war-torn populated Europe
- Peaceful emergence in relatively empty land, not through conquering established kingdoms
- Stark contrast to first beast rising from densely populated Mediterranean/European "sea"

**3. Two Horns Like a Lamb (Two Founding Principles)**:
- **Horn 1 - Civil Liberty (Republicanism)**: Representative government, Constitution limiting power, separation of powers (checks and balances), "government of the people, by the people, for the people"
- **Horn 2 - Religious Freedom**: First Amendment ("Congress shall make no law respecting an establishment of religion, or prohibiting the free exercise thereof"), no state church, freedom of conscience, separation of church and state
- **"Like a lamb"**: Appeared gentle, Christian, benevolent, peaceful, granting rights/freedoms - founding principles appeared lamb-like in stark contrast to oppressive church-state union of medieval Europe
- Nation became haven for religious refugees fleeing persecution
- Constitutional government protecting individual liberty
- Appeared as God's answer to centuries of papal tyranny

**4. Spoke Like a Dragon (Future Prophetic Warning)**:
- **Revelation 13:11**: "Spoke like a dragon"
- Despite lamb-like appearance, will speak dragon's message
- **Dragon** = Satan (Revelation 12:9)
- **Dragon's agenda**: Enforce worship contrary to God's commandments
- Nation founded on **religious freedom** will enforce **religious observance**
- **Prophetic irony**: Will abandon founding principle of religious freedom to enforce Sunday worship
- Will repeat Constantine's pattern: civil law enforcing religious practice
- Current Sunday initiatives moving steadily toward fulfillment

**The Second Beast's Future Actions (Revelation 13:12-17)**:

**Verse 12** - "Exercises all the authority of the first beast":
- Will wield papal-type power (church-state union authority)
- **"Causes the earth and those who dwell in it to worship the first beast"**
- Enforces papal teachings (Sunday observance) through civil law

**Verse 13** - "Performs great signs":
- Miracles, wonders, supernatural signs to deceive
- Appearance of divine approval on religious-civil alliance

**Verse 14** - **"Make an image to the beast"**:
- **Image** = Likeness, copy, replica
- Creates church-state union **mirroring** papal Rome's medieval system
- Protestant churches + U.S. government = Same structure as Catholic Church + Roman Empire
- Not the papacy itself, but Protestant America **acting like** the papacy

**Verse 15** - "Give breath to the image... cause to be killed":
- Image will **"speak"** (pass legislation)
- Enforce Sunday worship
- Eventually death decree for refusers

**Verses 16-17** - **The Mark of the Beast Enforced**:
> "He causes all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and slave, to receive **a mark on their right hand or on their foreheads**, and that **no one may buy or sell except one who has the mark** or the name of the beast, or the number of his name."

- **Mark** = Sign of allegiance/loyalty
| **Forehead** | Mind/Belief/Conscious choice | Deuteronomy 6:6-8; 11:18: God's Word "as frontlets between your eyes" (in the mind); Revelation 13:16; 14:9: Mark received on forehead = intellectual acceptance/belief |
| **Hand** | Actions/Works/Compliance | Deuteronomy 6:8; 11:18: God's Word "as a sign on your hand" (in actions); Revelation 13:16; 14:9: Mark on hand = outward compliance in conduct/work regardless of belief |
- **Economic enforcement**: Cannot buy/sell without accepting Sunday observance
- Second beast (USA) **enforces** the mark of first beast (papal Sunday)

**What Does "Image to the Beast" Mean Biblically?**

An **image** in biblical prophecy means a **likeness, copy, or reflection** - something that mirrors the characteristics and structure of the original. When Revelation 13:14 says the second beast will "make an image to the beast," it means the United States will **replicate the same system** that characterized the first beast (papal Rome).

**The First Beast's Defining Characteristic**:
- **Church + State union**: Vatican is both a religious authority (Catholic Church) AND a political state (Vatican City)
- Religious power wielding civil enforcement
- Spiritual authority backed by governmental law
- Church doctrines enforced through state legislation

**The Image to the Beast**:
- **United States creating the same Church + State union**
- Protestant churches + U.S. Government working together
- Religious doctrines enforced through civil law
- Spiritual authority (churches) using governmental power (legislation) to enforce Sunday observance

**Biblical Definition of "Image"**:

> "And he deceives those who dwell on the earth by those signs which he was granted to do in the sight of the beast, telling those who dwell on the earth to **make an image to the beast** who was wounded by the sword and lived." (Revelation 13:14)

The word "image" (Greek: *eikon*) means:
- **Likeness or resemblance**: A representation that mirrors the original
- **Copy or replica**: Not the original, but functions the same way
- **Reflection of character**: Possesses the same defining qualities

**How the Image Mirrors the Beast**:

| **First Beast (Papal Rome)** | **Image to the Beast (USA Church-State Union)** |
|------------------------------|------------------------------------------------|
| Church + State combined (Vatican) | Protestant churches + U.S. Government alliance |
| Religious authority makes laws | Religious coalition influences legislation |
| Enforced Sunday observance (medieval) | Will enforce Sunday observance (future) |
| Persecuted Sabbath-keepers | Will persecute Sabbath-keepers |
| Used civil power to enforce doctrine | Will use civil power to enforce doctrine |
| Constantine's 321 CE Sunday law | Future U.S. national Sunday law |
| Catholic Church + Roman Empire | Protestant churches + American government |

**Key Point**: The "image" is **not the Catholic Church itself** in America, but rather **Protestant churches adopting the same church-state enforcement model** that characterized papal Rome. Just as the Vatican combined religious authority with political power, so the United States will combine Protestant religious influence with governmental legislative power to enforce Sunday laws.

**Why This is Called an "Image"**:

1. **It mirrors the structure**: Church + State union (like the original beast)
2. **It copies the method**: Using civil law to enforce religious observance
3. **It reflects the character**: Religious authority persecuting those who refuse
4. **It's a different entity**: Not the papacy itself, but Protestant America acting like the papacy
5. **Same result**: Mandatory Sunday observance enforced by law with penalties

**The Prophetic Warning**:

The nation founded on **religious freedom** (separation of church and state) will abandon its founding principle and create an **image** - a replica church-state system - mirroring the very papal power from which it originally provided escape. Protestant churches, which once fled Catholic persecution in Europe, will **repeat the same pattern** by using government power to enforce their religious traditions.

**Historical Parallel**:
- **Medieval Europe**: Catholic Church + European governments = Enforced Sunday, persecuted Sabbath-keepers
- **Future America**: Protestant churches + U.S. Government = Will enforce Sunday, will persecute Sabbath-keepers
- **Same system, different players**: The "image" replicates the original beast's church-state union

**Scripture Confirms**:
> "He was granted power to give breath to the image of the beast, that the image of the beast should both speak and cause as many as would not worship the image of the beast to be killed." (Revelation 13:15)

The image will:
- **Speak** = Legislative action, laws, decrees
- **Cause worship** = Mandatory observance enforced by law
- **Persecute refusers** = Economic sanctions, legal penalties, eventually death decree

**Current Evidence of Transition**:
- **Project 2025** (USA) - Framework for "Christian nation" policies
- **Sunday blue laws** - Still enforced in many U.S. states
- Religious right political influence seeking to legislate morality
- Environmental justifications for mandatory rest days
- "Traditional values" rhetoric masking religious enforcement

**For detailed documentation of:**
- **Image of the Beast forming** (church-state separation breakdown): See [Project 2025 / Heritage Foundation](#1-project-2025--heritage-foundation---sunday-implicit) section in Part IV
- **Sunday law initiatives**: See [Global Sunday Rest Convergence](#global-sunday-rest-convergence) in Part IV: Contemporary Fulfillment (2024-2026)

**The Lamb Symbolism in Prophecy**

**True Lamb (Jesus Christ)**:
- **John 1:29**: "Behold! The Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world!"
- **Characteristics**: Innocent, perfect sacrifice, voluntary death, blood saves from sin
- **Gives freedom**: Never forces worship, died to liberate
- **Revelation 5:6-12**: Worthy of worship, redeemed humanity by His blood

**False Lamb (Second Beast)**:
- **Revelation 13:11**: "Two horns like a lamb... spoke like a dragon"
- **Appearance**: Lamb-like (Christian, gentle, promotes liberty)
- **Reality**: Dragon's voice (enforces satanic agenda against God's law)
- **Deception**: Religious appearance hiding anti-biblical intent
- **Forces worship**: Causes earth to worship first beast through legislation

**Connection to Sabbath Change**

The United States' prophesied role in enforcing Sunday observance represents the culmination of the Sabbath change that began with Constantine in 321 CE:

**Historical Pattern**:
1. **321 CE**: Constantine makes Sunday rest civil law (political power enforcing religious change)
2. **364 CE**: Council of Laodicea bans Saturday Sabbath (church authority enforcing change)
3. **538-1798 CE**: Papal persecution of Saturday Sabbath-keepers (1,260 years of enforcement)

**For detailed historical documentation**: See [Persecution: Past, Present, and Future](#persecution-past-present-and-future) in Part V for comprehensive evidence of the 1,260-year persecution period, including Inquisitions, Waldensian massacres, and martyrdom of Sabbath-keepers.

4. **1798**: Papal deadly wound - persecution power temporarily broken
5. **1776-1798**: United States rises with religious liberty principles
6. **Future**: United States will enforce Sunday law globally - repeating history

**The Warning**:
Just as the papacy changed the Sabbath from Saturday to Sunday by human authority, the United States - founded as an escape from religious tyranny - will enforce this same change through civil law. The prophecy reveals that appealing to "family values," "tradition," "worker protection," and "environmental sustainability," the lamb-like nation will speak with the dragon's voice, making Sunday observance mandatory and persecuting those who keep God's true seventh-day Sabbath.

**Revelation 14:9-12** - The Final Warning:
> "If anyone worships the beast and his image, and receives his mark on his forehead or on his hand, he himself shall also drink of the wine of the wrath of God... Here is the patience of the saints; here are those who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus."

The final conflict centers on **worship** and **God's commandments** - specifically, the fourth commandment identifying the seventh-day Sabbath. Those who follow the true Lamb (Jesus) will keep His commandments despite persecution. Those who follow the false lamb (enforced Sunday worship) will receive the mark of the beast.

**Interesting Note: Catholic Influence in U.S. Supreme Court**

As of February 2026, **6 out of 9 U.S. Supreme Court justices are Catholic** (approximately 67%):

**Catholic Justices**:
1. **John Roberts** (Chief Justice) - Catholic
2. **Clarence Thomas** - Catholic (raised Protestant, converted to Catholicism)
3. **Samuel Alito** - Catholic
4. **Sonia Sotomayor** - Catholic
5. **Brett Kavanaugh** - Catholic
6. **Amy Coney Barrett** - Catholic

**Non-Catholic Justices**:
7. **Ketanji Brown Jackson** - Protestant (non-denominational)
8. **Elena Kagan** - Jewish
9. **Neil Gorsuch** - Raised Catholic, now attends Episcopal Church (unclear identification)

**Historical Context**:
- Catholics represent approximately **20-23% of U.S. population**
- Yet comprise **67% of the Supreme Court**
- This is the **highest Catholic representation** in Supreme Court history
- First Catholic justice appointed: **Roger Taney** (1836)
- Until 1980s, typically only 1-2 Catholic justices at most
- Sharp increase beginning in 1990s-2000s

**Prophetic Significance**:
While judicial decisions are made on constitutional grounds, this unprecedented Catholic majority on the nation's highest court is noteworthy given the prophecy that the United States (the "lamb-like beast") will eventually enforce the "mark of the beast" (Sunday observance) in cooperation with papal authority (the "first beast"). The U.S. Supreme Court would ultimately decide the constitutionality of any federal Sunday law, making the religious composition of the Court particularly significant in understanding potential future enforcement mechanisms.

**Important Note**: This observation is not meant to question the integrity or qualifications of individual justices, but rather to note the remarkable shift in religious demographics at the highest level of U.S. judicial authority—a shift that aligns with the prophetic prediction of increasing Catholic influence in American institutions as the nation transitions from "lamb-like" (religious freedom) to "speaking like a dragon" (religious enforcement).

And I saw a **woman sitting on a scarlet beast** which was full of names of blasphemy, having seven heads and ten horns. The woman was **arrayed in purple and scarlet, and adorned with gold and precious stones and pearls**, having in her hand a golden cup full of abominations and the filthiness of her fornication. And on her forehead a name was written: **MYSTERY, BABYLON THE GREAT, THE MOTHER OF HARLOTS AND OF THE ABOMINATIONS OF THE EARTH**."

| **Drunk with wine of fornication** | Revelation 17:2; 18:3 | False doctrines intoxicating nations (Sunday, immortal soul, etc.) |

| **"BABYLON THE GREAT"** | Revelation 17:5 | Confusion - mixing biblical truth with pagan traditions |
| **"MOTHER OF HARLOTS"** | Revelation 17:5 | Protestant churches (daughters) broke from Rome but retained multiple Catholic doctrines without biblical basis: Sunday worship (changed from biblical seventh-day Sabbath), infant baptism (Bible shows believer's baptism by choice), immortal soul (Greek philosophy, not Scripture - Bible teaches soul dies), eternal hellfire (pagan mythology - Bible teaches wicked are destroyed, not eternally tortured), Christmas/Easter (pagan festivals Christianized), church hierarchy over Scripture authority |
| **Drunk with saints' blood** | Revelation 17:6 | Inquisitions, martyrdom of Bible-believers, persecution of Sabbath-keepers |
| **Sits on seven mountains** | Revelation 17:9 | Rome, the city on seven hills (Septem Montes) |

- **Woman** (church) sits on and **directs** the **beast** (political power)

#### **The Antichrist Connection (1 John, 2 Thessalonians)**

While "Antichrist" is not explicitly named in Daniel or Revelation's beast prophecies, **1 John and 2 Thessalonians** provide additional characteristics that connect to the same power.

**1 John 2:18, 22**:
> "Little children, it is the last hour; and as you have heard that the **Antichrist is coming**, even now many antichrists have come... Who is a liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ? He is **antichrist** who denies the Father and the Son."

**1 John 4:3**:
> "Every spirit that does not confess that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is not of God. And this is the spirit of the **Antichrist**, which you have heard was coming, and **is now already in the world**."

**2 Thessalonians 2:3-4**:
> "Let no one deceive you by any means; for that Day will not come unless the falling away comes first, and **the man of sin is revealed, the son of perdition**, who **opposes and exalts himself above all that is called God** or that is worshiped, so that **he sits as God in the temple of God, showing himself that he is God**."

**Understanding "Antichrist"**:

The Greek prefix "anti" (ἀντί) means **two things**:
1. **Against** - opposition to Christ
2. **In place of** - substituting for Christ, taking Christ's position

The Antichrist is not merely someone who opposes Christ, but one who **takes Christ's place**—claiming His titles, authority, and prerogatives while leading people away from biblical truth.

**Antichrist Characteristics = Beast from the Sea (Papacy)**:

| **Antichrist Trait** | **Biblical Reference** | **Beast/Papal Fulfillment** |
|---------------------|----------------------|----------------------------|
| **Exalts himself above God** | 2 Thessalonians 2:4 | Papal infallibility, titles like "Lord God the Pope" |
| **Sits as God in temple** | 2 Thessalonians 2:4 | Pope claims Christ's position as head of Church on earth |
| **Shows himself that he is God** | 2 Thessalonians 2:4 | "Holy Father" (God's title), "Vicar of Christ" (Christ's substitute) |
| **Man of sin/lawlessness** | 2 Thessalonians 2:3 | Changed God's law (removed 2nd commandment, altered 4th Sabbath commandment) |
| **Spirit of Antichrist already in world** | 1 John 4:3 | System emerged in early church, formalized by Constantine era |
| **Claims to speak for God** | Implied in context | Papal decrees treated as equal to Scripture, tradition above Bible |

**The Connection**:
- **Daniel 7**: Little horn = Political-religious power changing law, persecuting saints
- **Revelation 13**: Beast from sea = Same power with blasphemous names, 1,260-year authority
- **Revelation 17**: Woman on beast = Apostate church controlling political powers
- **1 John/2 Thessalonians**: Antichrist = One who takes Christ's place, exalts self as God
- **All describe the same entity**: **Papal system** - church-state power claiming divine authority, changing God's law, persecuting believers

**Not a Future Individual, But a Present System**:

Many expect a future individual called "the Antichrist." However, Scripture indicates:
- **"Is now already in the world"** (1 John 4:3) - Present in John's time, continuing
- **"Mystery of lawlessness already at work"** (2 Thessalonians 2:7) - Operating in Paul's time
- Describes a **system** (religious-political power) over centuries, not a single person
- The papacy has functioned "in place of Christ" for over 1,500 years

#### **Summary: Four Prophetic Views of the Same Power**

| **Prophecy** | **Symbol** | **Focus** | **Key Identifying Mark** |
|-------------|-----------|----------|-------------------------|
| **Daniel 7** | **Little horn** among ten kingdoms | Historical succession and law-changing power | Changes "times and law" (Sabbath to Sunday) |
| **Revelation 13:1-10** | **Beast from the sea** | Blasphemous authority and persecution (1,260 years) | Speaks blasphemies, makes war with saints, receives deadly wound |
| **Revelation 13:11-18** | **Beast from the earth** | End-time enforcement power | Enforces mark of first beast (Sunday law) |
| **Revelation 17** | **Woman on beast** (Babylon) | Apostate church controlling nations | Drunk with saints' blood, fornication with kings, seven hills |
| **2 Thessalonians 2** | **Man of sin / Antichrist** | Religious leader claiming divine authority | Sits as God, exalts above God, opposes God |

**All Five Prophecies Converge on**:
1. **Papal Rome** (first beast/little horn/woman/Antichrist) - Changed Sabbath, persecuted saints 1,260 years
2. **United States** (second beast) - Will enforce papal Sunday law through civil legislation
3. **The Issue**: God's seventh-day Sabbath (seal of God) vs. papal Sunday (mark of the beast)
4. **The Test**: Will you obey God's commandments or submit to human religious authority?

**Key Principle**: Daniel provides the **historical framework** (four kingdoms → divided Rome → little horn); Revelation adds **spiritual warfare details** (two beasts, mark of the beast, seal of God, final test of worship); John and Paul identify the **spiritual character** (Antichrist taking Christ's place). All converge on the **same issue**: Will you obey God's commandments (including Sabbath) or submit to human authority (Sunday tradition)?
