#### **The Protestant Reformers' Unanimous Testimony: The Papacy Is Antichrist**

**Historical Protestant Consensus (1517-1800s)**:

For over 300 years, **every major Protestant reformer and Protestant confession of faith** identified the papal system as the Antichrist prophesied in Scripture. This was not a peripheral issue—it was **central to Protestant identity** and the Reformation itself.

**The Reformers Spoke With One Voice**:

**Martin Luther (1483-1546)** - Father of the Reformation:
> "We here are of the conviction that the papacy is the seat of the true and real Antichrist... personally I declare that I owe the Pope no other obedience than that to Antichrist."

> "The pope is the very Antichrist who has exalted himself above and opposed himself against Christ, because he will not permit Christians to be saved without his power."

Luther identified the pope as Antichrist and the papal throne as **Satan's seat**. This conviction drove the entire Reformation.

**John Calvin (1509-1564)** - Founder of Reformed Theology:
> "Some persons think us too severe and censorious when we call the Roman pontiff Antichrist. But those who are of this opinion do not consider that they bring the same charge of presumption against Paul himself, after whom we speak and whose language we adopt... I shall briefly show that (Paul's words in 2 Thessalonians 2) are not capable of any other interpretation than that which applies them to the Papacy."

Calvin defended calling the pope Antichrist using the Apostle Paul's own language. He **denied the pope was the vicar or head of the church**, explicitly calling him Antichrist.

**John Knox (1505-1572)** - Scottish Reformer:
> "That tyranny which the pope himself has for so many ages exercised over the church... **the very antichrist, and son of perdition, of whom Paul speaks**."

Knox argued for the removal of papal tyranny, identifying the Pope as "**the very antichrist, and son of perdition**" prophesied by Paul in 2 Thessalonians 2:3.

**Thomas Cranmer (1489-1556)** - Archbishop of Canterbury, English Reformation:
> "Whereof it followeth Rome to be the seat of antichrist, and the pope to be very antichrist himself. I could prove the same by many other scriptures, old writers, and strong reasons."

Cranmer, interpreting biblical prophecy, concluded that **Rome was the seat of Antichrist** and **the Pope was Antichrist himself**.

**Philipp Melanchthon (1497-1560)** - Luther's Closest Associate, Reformer:
> "Since it is certain that the pontiff and his kingdom is the Antichrist, his tyranny must be destroyed... This is the true meaning of the prophecy given in these passages which testify that the Antichrist would be the potentate in the Church who would be an adversary of Christ."

Melanchthon clearly stated that **the Roman pontiff, with his system, was the Antichrist**.

**Protestant Confessional Statements - Official Church Doctrine**:

The identification of the papacy as Antichrist was so fundamental to Protestant theology that it was **written into their official confessions of faith**:

**1. Westminster Confession of Faith (1646)** - Presbyterian/Reformed Standard:

**Chapter 25, Section 6**:
> "There is no other head of the Church but the Lord Jesus Christ. Nor can the Pope of Rome, in any sense, be head thereof; **but is that Antichrist, that man of sin, and son of perdition, that exalts himself, in the Church, against Christ and all that is called God**."

The Westminster Confession—still used by Presbyterian and Reformed churches worldwide—declares the Pope is:
- **"That Antichrist"**
- **"That man of sin"** (2 Thessalonians 2:3)
- **"Son of perdition"** (2 Thessalonians 2:3)
- One who **"exalts himself... against Christ"**

**2. London Baptist Confession (1677/1689)** - Baptist Standard:

**Chapter 26, Section 4**:
> "The Lord Jesus Christ is the Head of the church, in whom, by the appointment of the Father, all power for the calling, institution, order or government of the church, is invested in a supreme and sovereign manner; neither can the Pope of Rome in any sense be head thereof, **but is that antichrist, that man of sin, and son of perdition, that exalteth himself in the church against Christ, and all that is called God**; whom the Lord shall destroy with the brightness of his coming."

Identical language to Westminster—Baptists agreed the papacy was the prophesied Antichrist system.

**3. Smalcald Articles (1537)** - Lutheran Standard:

Written by Martin Luther, adopted as part of the Lutheran Book of Concord:

**Part II, Article IV, Section 10**:
> "This teaching [of papal supremacy] shows forcefully that **the Pope is the very Antichrist, who has exalted himself above, and opposed himself against Christ** because he will not permit Christians to be saved without his power, which, nevertheless, is nothing, and is neither ordained nor commanded by God."

Lutheran confessional doctrine explicitly identifies the pope as **"the very Antichrist"** based on his exaltation above Christ and opposition to Christ's authority.

**4. Thirty-Nine Articles of Religion (1563)** - Anglican/Episcopal Standard:

**Article XIX** (On the Church):
While not as explicit as others, Anglican theology historically identified the papacy as Antichrist. The Book of Homilies (official Anglican sermons) taught this openly.

**Why the Reformers Unanimously Held This View**:

The Reformers identified the papacy as Antichrist based on specific biblical criteria:

1. **2 Thessalonians 2:3-4** - "Man of sin... exalts himself above all that is called God... sits as God in the temple"
   - **Papal fulfillment**: Pope claims infallibility, sits in church as Christ's vicar, receives worship

2. **Daniel 7:25** - "Shall speak pompous words... intend to change times and law"
   - **Papal fulfillment**: Changed Sabbath commandment from Saturday to Sunday

3. **Revelation 13:5-7** - Speaks blasphemies, makes war with saints, rules 1,260 years
   - **Papal fulfillment**: Blasphemous titles ("Holy Father," "Lord God the Pope"), Inquisition persecution, dominated Europe 538-1798

4. **1 John 2:18, 4:3** - "Antichrist... is now already in the world"
   - **Papal fulfillment**: System emerged in early church, consolidated by Constantine, formalized by papal supremacy

**Not Anti-Catholic People, But Anti-Papal System**:

The Reformers **did not hate Catholic people**—they were calling **Catholic believers out of a false system**. They identified the **papal office and system** as Antichrist, not individual Catholics. Many Reformers (Luther, Calvin, Knox) were **themselves Catholic** before seeing the biblical truth.

**The Modern Abandonment of This Biblical Truth**:

**What Changed?**

Beginning in the 1800s and accelerating in the 1900s, Protestant churches **abandoned** their historic identification of the papacy as Antichrist:

**1. Ecumenical Movement (1900s)**:
- Push for Catholic-Protestant unity
- Identifying the pope as Antichrist became "offensive" and "unloving"
- Doctrine sacrificed for perceived unity

**2. Futurism and Preterism**:
- **Futurism**: Jesuit Counter-Reformation interpretation—Antichrist is future individual, not papacy
- **Preterism**: Jesuit interpretation—Antichrist was Nero, prophecies already fulfilled
- **Both deflect attention from papacy**

**3. Dispensationalism (1800s)**:
- John Nelson Darby's new system emphasized future Antichrist
- Popularized by Scofield Reference Bible (1909)
- Spread by evangelical seminaries and media

**4. Political Pressure**:
- Catholic voting bloc in America
- Interfaith dialogue initiatives
- Cultural pressure to be "tolerant"

**The Result**:

**Modern Protestant churches**:
- Removed Antichrist identification from confessions or ignore them
- Teach futuristic Antichrist (one evil man in the future)
- Partner with Vatican on social/political issues
- **Forgotten their own confessional doctrine**

**Presbyterian churches** still officially hold Westminster Confession—but most don't teach it.

**Baptist churches** still officially hold London Baptist Confession—but most ignore it.

**Lutheran churches** still officially hold Book of Concord—but rarely preach it.

**Result**: Protestant churches **drank more of Babylon's wine**—forgot their prophetic foundation and returned to partnership with the system their fathers identified as Antichrist.

**Why This Matters Today**:

The **abandonment** of the Reformers' biblical identification of the papacy as Antichrist has led directly to:

1. **Ecumenical Sunday Law Support**: Protestants now partner with Vatican on Sunday rest initiatives (see Project 2025, European Sunday Alliance)

2. **Loss of Prophetic Understanding**: Modern Protestants don't understand Revelation 13-14 because they don't see papal system as the beast

3. **Compromise on Sabbath**: If papacy isn't Antichrist who changed God's law, why resist Sunday tradition?

4. **Unprepared for Final Test**: When Sunday laws come, Protestants won't recognize it as the mark of the beast because they've forgotten papal system is the beast

**The Reformers Were Right**:

Every characteristic the Reformers identified remains true today:
- ✓ Papacy still claims to be Christ's vicar (in place of Christ)
- ✓ Pope still claims infallibility (speaking as God)
- ✓ Papacy still enforces Sunday (changed God's law)
- ✓ Vatican still claims authority over all churches
- ✓ Papacy still sits in church claiming Christ's position

**The Reformers saw it clearly. Modern churches have forgotten. God's final warning in Revelation 14 calls Protestants to remember their heritage and "come out" of Babylon before it's too late.**

**Key Point**: The Protestant Reformation was built on the biblical identification of the papal system as the prophesied Antichrist. Every major reformer, every Protestant confession, unanimously testified to this truth for 300 years. The modern abandonment of this doctrine is itself evidence of Babylon's wine—Protestant churches drinking Catholic teaching, forgetting their biblical foundation, and returning to partnership with the system Scripture identifies as the beast. When Sunday laws are enforced, those who have forgotten this history will not recognize the mark of the beast being implemented before their eyes.

### **Why Vatican Represents Continuation of Fourth Beast**

#### **1. Geographic Continuity**
- Vatican City is located in **Rome**, the capital of the fourth kingdom
- Occupies the same geographic and political space as ancient Roman Empire
- Papal residence at Vatican Hill since 4th century CE
- Inherits Roman imperial symbolism and titles

#### **2. Religious-Political Fusion**
- **Only entity in the world** that is simultaneously both church and state
- Pope serves as both religious leader and head of state
- Issues both theological decrees and political treaties
- Maintains diplomatic corps and signs international agreements
- Has own legal system, currency, passports, and courts

#### **3. Claims Universal Authority**
- Papal title "Pontifex Maximus" (Supreme Pontiff) - same title as Roman emperors
- Claims jurisdiction over all Christians worldwide
- Asserts authority to interpret Scripture for all believers
- Declares papal infallibility in matters of faith and morals
- Like Rome claimed to rule the known world, Vatican claims spiritual rule over all Christendom

#### **4. Changed God's Law**
- **Daniel 7:25 prophecy**: The power would "intend to change times and law"
- Vatican altered **God's Ten Commandments** in three specific ways:
  - **Removed the second commandment**: "You shall not make graven images" (Exodus 20:4-6) - enables statue and icon worship
  - **Changed the fourth commandment**: Sabbath from Saturday (seventh day) to Sunday (first day) - replaces God's holy day with human tradition
  - **Split the tenth commandment**: Divided one covetousness command into two separate commandments to maintain the count of ten after removing the second
- Changed "times" (day of worship from Saturday to Sunday) and "law" (God's commandments themselves)
- Catholic Church openly acknowledges making these changes by its own authority

**Catholic Acknowledgment**:
> "The Church changed the observance of the Sabbath to Sunday by right of the divine, infallible authority given to her by her Founder, Jesus Christ. The Protestant claiming the Bible to be the only guide of faith, has no warrant for observing Sunday." (*The Catholic Universe Bulletin*, August 14, 1942)

**Biblical Warning**:
> "You shall not add to the word which I command you, nor take from it, that you may keep the commandments of the LORD your God which I command you." (Deuteronomy 4:2)

> "For assuredly, I say to you, till heaven and earth pass away, one jot or one tittle will by no means pass from the law till all is fulfilled." (Matthew 5:18)

#### **5. Persecuted the Saints**
- **Daniel 7:25**: "shall persecute the saints of the Most High"
- Spanish Inquisition (1478-1834): Executed thousands for heresy
- Medieval persecution of Waldensians, Albigensians, and Saturday Sabbath keepers
- Prosecution of Seventh-day Adventists, Seventh Day Baptists (documented in this study)
- 1,600+ years of persecution for those who maintained biblical Saturday Sabbath
- Methods: execution, imprisonment, torture, property confiscation, social ostracism

#### **6. Time Period Alignment**
- **Daniel 7:25**: Power would persecute saints for "a time, times, and half a time" (3.5 prophetic years = 1,260 prophetic days = 1,260 literal years using day-year principle)
- Papal supremacy established: ~538 CE (Justinian's decree)
- Papal temporal power lost: 1798 CE (Napoleon's imprisonment of Pope Pius VI)
- **Duration**: 1,260 years (538-1798 CE) - matches Daniel's prophecy
- Vatican City restored as sovereign state: 1929 CE (Lateran Treaty) - "deadly wound was healed" (Revelation 13:3)

#### **7. Ten Horns/Toes - Kings Give Power to the Beast**

**Daniel 7:24**: "The ten horns are ten kings who shall arise from this kingdom"

**Revelation 17:12-14** - The Kings Who Gave Their Power to the Beast:
> "The ten horns which you saw are ten kings who have received no kingdom as yet, but they receive authority for one hour as kings with the beast. **These are of one mind, and they will give their power and authority to the beast. These will make war with the Lamb, and the Lamb will overcome them**, for He is Lord of lords and King of kings; and those who are with Him are called, chosen, and faithful."

**Historical Fulfillment**:
- Western Roman Empire divided into ten kingdoms of Europe (476 CE)
- These kingdoms **gave their power and authority to the beast** (papal Rome)
- Catholic kingdoms supported papal supremacy religiously, politically, and militarily
- Kings enforced papal decrees, Sunday laws, and persecution against "heretics"
- Executed Inquisition orders, burned Bible believers, imprisoned Sabbath-keepers
- The "little horn" (Daniel 7:8, 24-25) arose among these kingdoms = Papacy

**They Made War with the Lamb**:
- European kingdoms, empowered by papal authority, persecuted those who followed the **Word of God**
- **The Lamb = Jesus Christ = The Word** (John 1:1, 14: "In the beginning was the Word, and the Word was with God, and the Word was God... And the Word became flesh")
- Burned Bibles, banned Scripture translation into common languages
- Executed those who distributed Scripture (William Tyndale, John Wycliffe's bones exhumed and burned)
- Martyred believers who held to biblical truth over church tradition

**The Lamb Triumphed Through the Reformation**:
- **Revelation 17:14**: "The Lamb will overcome them, for He is Lord of lords and King of kings"
- **How the Lamb overcame**: Through His **Word** - Scripture translated, printed, and distributed
- **Protestant Reformation (16th century)**: The Word of God broke papal dominance
  - **Martin Luther** (1517): Nailed 95 Theses, translated Bible into German - *sola scriptura* (Scripture alone)
  - **William Tyndale**: Translated Bible into English, martyred 1536 ("God's Word will stand forever")
  - **John Calvin, Ulrich Zwingli, John Knox**: Spread biblical truth across Europe
  - **Printing press** (Gutenberg, 1440): Multiplied Bibles, broke church's information monopoly
- **The Word exposed the beast**: Bible in common languages revealed papal errors
  - Showed Sunday has no biblical warrant (Sabbath is seventh day)
  - Exposed indulgences, purgatory, praying to saints as unbiblical
  - Revealed Jesus as sole Mediator (1 Timothy 2:5), not pope or priests
- **1798 CE - Deadly wound**: Napoleon imprisoned Pope Pius VI, ended 1,260-year persecution period
- **Victory of the Word**: Where Scripture was available, reformation triumphed; where suppressed, darkness remained

**Key Point**: The same **kingdoms** (ten horns/toes) that gave power to the beast are now the **European nations** where Vatican still exerts influence (iron-clay mixture). But the **Lamb** (Jesus, the living Word) triumphed through the **written Word** (Scripture), and will triumph again at His return.

**Modern Application**:
- Vatican maintains diplomatic influence across all European nations
- European Sunday Alliance pressures EU governments on Sunday rest laws
- Same pattern repeating: Religious authority using political power to enforce worship
- But **the Word of God endures forever** (Isaiah 40:8; 1 Peter 1:25) - truth will prevail

#### **8. The Antichrist: "In Place of" Christ**

**Understanding "Antichrist"**:

The Greek prefix "anti" (ἀντί) has two meanings:
1. **Against** - opposition to Christ
2. **In place of** - substituting for Christ, claiming Christ's position

The biblical antichrist is not merely someone who opposes Christ, but one who **takes the place of Christ** - claiming His titles, authority, and prerogatives while leading people away from biblical truth.

**Biblical Identification**:

**1 John 2:18, 22**:
> "Little children, it is the last hour; and as you have heard that the **Antichrist is coming**, even now many antichrists have come... Who is a liar but he who denies that Jesus is the Christ? He is **antichrist** who denies the Father and the Son."

**2 Thessalonians 2:3-4**:
> "Let no one deceive you by any means; for that Day will not come unless the falling away comes first, and **the man of sin is revealed, the son of perdition, who opposes and exalts himself above all that is called God** or that is worshiped, so that **he sits as God in the temple of God, showing himself that he is God**."

**1 John 4:3**:
> "Every spirit that does not confess that Jesus Christ has come in the flesh is not of God. And this is the spirit of the **Antichrist**, which you have heard was coming, and is now already in the world."

#### **Seven Biblical Criteria of Antichrist - Fulfilled by the Papacy**

| **Criterion** | **Biblical Basis** | **Papal Fulfillment** |
|--------------|-------------------|---------------------|
| **1. Blasphemous Speech** | Revelation 13:5-6: "mouth speaking great things and blasphemies... he opened his mouth in blasphemy against God" | Papal titles: "Holy Father" (only God - Matthew 23:9), "Vicar of Christ" (Christ's substitute), claims to forgive sins (only God can - Mark 2:7), papal infallibility (only God is infallible) |
| **2. False Messiah (In Place of Christ)** | 2 Thessalonians 2:4: "sits as God in the temple of God, showing himself that he is God" | Pope claims to be "Vicar of the Son of God" (*Vicarius Filii Dei*), sits in position of Christ on earth, called "another God on earth" in Catholic documents, requires obedience as to Christ |
| **3. Economic Control** | Revelation 13:16-17: "no one may buy or sell except one who has the mark" | Medieval church controlled commerce through Sunday laws and holy day requirements, excommunication meant economic ruin (couldn't buy/sell/work), future enforcement of Sunday laws with economic penalties |
| **4. Claim to Divinity** | 2 Thessalonians 2:4: "exalts himself above all that is called God" | Pope Innocent III: "The pope is not simply a man but as it were God, and God's vicar"; Pope Leo XIII: "We hold upon this earth the place of God Almighty"; Titles like "His Holiness" reserved for God alone |
| **5. Political Power** | Daniel 7:24-25: "shall subdue three kings... change times and law" | Papal States ruled for over 1,000 years, crowned/deposed kings, "power over all kings" claimed, diplomatic relations with 180+ nations, influenced governments throughout history, three kingdoms destroyed (Heruli, Vandals, Ostrogoths) |
| **6. Lawlessness (Changes God's Law)** | Daniel 7:25: "think to change times and law"; 2 Thessalonians 2:3: "man of sin" (lawless one) | Changed Ten Commandments (removed 2nd, altered 4th, split 10th), changed Sabbath from Saturday to Sunday, tradition elevated above Scripture, openly admits to changing God's law by church authority |
| **7. Persecution of Saints** | Revelation 13:7: "make war with the saints"; Daniel 7:25: "wear out the saints of the Most High" | Inquisitions killed millions, Waldensian massacres, persecution of Sabbath-keepers, 1,260 years of papal persecution (538-1798 CE), torture and execution for "heresy" (holding biblical truth). See [Persecution: Past, Present, and Future](#persecution-past-present-and-future) for comprehensive documentation. |

#### **Detailed Evidence for Each Criterion**

**1. Blasphemous Speech**

**What is Blasphemy?**
- **Mark 2:7**: "Who can forgive sins but God alone?" (claiming to forgive sins = blasphemy)
- **John 10:33**: "You, being a Man, make Yourself God" (claiming divine prerogatives = blasphemy)
- **Matthew 23:9**: "Do not call anyone on earth your father; for One is your Father, He who is in heaven" (taking God's title = blasphemy)

**Papal Blasphemies**:
- **"Holy Father"** - Title used for God alone (John 17:11: Jesus calls God "Holy Father")
- **Claims to forgive sins** - Catholic confession requires absolution from priest/pope
- **"Vicar of Christ"** (*Vicarius Christi*) - Claims to be Christ's substitute on earth
- **Papal infallibility** - Claims to speak without error in matters of faith (attribute of God alone)
- **"Lord God the Pope"** - Used in Catholic canon law (Extravagantes of Pope John XXII, title 14, chapter 4)

**2. False Messiah: "In Place of" Christ**

**Vicar = Substitute/Replacement**:
- Pope claims to be **"Vicar of the Son of God"** (*Vicarius Filii Dei*)
- Takes Christ's position as Head of Church on earth
- Mediator between God and man (contradicts 1 Timothy 2:5: "one Mediator... Christ Jesus")

**Catholic Teaching**:
> "The Pope is of so great dignity and so exalted that he is not a mere man, but as it were God, and the vicar of God... The Pope is of such lofty and supreme dignity that, properly speaking, he has not been established in any rank of dignity, but rather has been placed upon the very summit of all ranks of dignities... The Pope is as it were God on earth, sole sovereign of the faithful of Christ, chief king of kings, having plenitude of power." (*Ferraris Ecclesiastical Dictionary*, article "Pope")

**3. Economic Control**

**Historical Control**:
- Medieval church controlled commerce through compulsory Sunday observance
- Holy day violations resulted in fines, loss of business licenses
- Excommunication = economic death (couldn't buy, sell, conduct business, or hold property)
- Indulgences system monetized salvation

**Prophetic Future Control**:
- **Revelation 13:16-17**: "No one may buy or sell except one who has the mark"
- Sunday laws will have economic penalties (documented in "Global Sunday Rest Convergence" section)
- Those refusing Sunday observance will be excluded from commerce
- Pattern already established in medieval period, being revived today

**4. Claim to Divinity**

**Pope Innocent III** (1198-1216):
> "The pope is not simply a man but as it were God, and God's vicar."

**Pope Leo XIII** (*The Great Encyclical Letters*, 1903):
> "We hold upon this earth the place of God Almighty."

**Pope Pius IX**:
> "I alone... am the successor of the apostles, the vicar of Jesus Christ. I am the way, the truth, and the life..."

**Lucius Ferraris** (*Prompta Bibliotheca*, 1763):
> "The Pope is of so great authority and power that he can modify, explain, or interpret even divine laws... The Pope can modify divine law, since his power is not of man but of God, and he acts as vicegerent of God upon earth."

**5. Political Power**

**Historical Political Dominance**:
- **Papal States** (754-1870 CE): Pope ruled as temporal king over large territory in Italy
- **Crowned emperors and kings**: Pope crowned Holy Roman Emperors, claimed authority to depose rulers
- **Subdued three kingdoms**: Heruli (493 CE), Vandals (534 CE), Ostrogoths (538 CE) - eliminated to establish papal supremacy

**Modern Political Power**:
- Diplomatic relations with 180+ nations
- Vatican City = sovereign nation-state since 1929 (Lateran Treaty)
- Pope functions as both religious leader and head of state
- Influences international policy (Sunday laws, climate agreements, economic policy)

**Daniel 7:24-25 Fulfillment**:
> "He shall subdue three kings" - Three Arian kingdoms destroyed to establish papal political power

**6. Lawlessness: Changes God's Law**

**2 Thessalonians 2:3**: "Man of sin" (Greek: *anomia* = lawlessness)

The antichrist is identified as **lawless** - not because he has no laws, but because he changes God's law.

**Daniel 7:25**: "Think to change times and law"

**Papal Changes to God's Ten Commandments**:
1. **REMOVED** 2nd Commandment: "You shall not make graven images" (Exodus 20:4-6)
2. **CHANGED** 4th Commandment: Sabbath from Saturday (seventh day) to Sunday (first day)
3. **SPLIT** 10th Commandment: Divided into two to maintain count of ten

**Catholic Admission**:
> "The Church... took the pagan Sunday and made it the Christian Sunday... The Church made a sacred day of Sunday... largely because it was the weekly festival of the sun; for it was a definite Christian policy to take over the pagan festivals endeared to the people by tradition, and to give them a Christian significance." (*Catholic World*, March 1894)

> "It is well to remind the Presbyterians, Baptists, Methodists, and all other Christians, that the Bible does not support them anywhere in their observance of Sunday. Sunday is an institution of the Roman Catholic Church, and those who observe the day observe a commandment of the Catholic Church." (*Priest Brady*, in *Elizabeth, New Jersey News*, March 18, 1903)

**7. Persecution of Saints**

**Revelation 13:7**: "Make war with the saints and to overcome them"
**Daniel 7:25**: "Wear out the saints of the Most High"

**Historical Persecution**:
- **Spanish Inquisition** (1478-1834): Tortured and executed thousands for "heresy"
- **Waldensian Massacres**: Entire communities destroyed for keeping Saturday Sabbath
- **Albigensian Crusade** (1209-1229): Estimated 1 million killed
- **St. Bartholomew's Day Massacre** (1572): 70,000 Protestants killed in France
- **Total estimate**: 50-100 million killed during 1,260-year papal supremacy (538-1798 CE)

**Methods of Persecution**:
- Torture (rack, strappado, water torture, burning)
- Execution (burning at stake, hanging, beheading)
- Property confiscation
- Imprisonment
- Social ostracism

**Modern Persecution**:
- Economic discrimination against Sabbath-keepers
- Future prophecy: Enforcement of Sunday law with death penalty (Revelation 13:15)

**For comprehensive documentation**: See [Persecution: Past, Present, and Future](#persecution-past-present-and-future) in Part V for detailed historical evidence, modern discrimination patterns, and prophesied future persecution.

#### **Conclusion: Perfect Prophetic Match**

The papacy is the **only institution in history** that fulfills **all seven biblical criteria** of the antichrist:

1. ✓ **Blasphemous Speech** - Claims titles and prerogatives of God
2. ✓ **False Messiah** - Takes Christ's place as "Vicar" on earth
3. ✓ **Economic Control** - Historical and future control of commerce through religious law
4. ✓ **Claim to Divinity** - Official Catholic statements call pope "as it were God on earth"
5. ✓ **Political Power** - Ruled Papal States, crowned emperors, diplomatic relations with nations
6. ✓ **Lawlessness** - Changed God's Ten Commandments by human authority
7. ✓ **Persecution** - 1,260 years of persecution, millions killed for maintaining biblical truth

This is not speculation or religious prejudice - it is **biblical identification** using the criteria Scripture provides. The antichrist is not a future individual to emerge, but a **system** that has been "in place of" Christ for over 1,500 years, leading billions away from biblical truth through counterfeit worship (Sunday instead of Sabbath) and false authority (tradition over Scripture).

**2 Thessalonians 2:7-8**:
> "For the mystery of lawlessness is already at work... And then the lawless one will be revealed, whom the Lord will consume with the breath of His mouth and destroy with the brightness of His coming."

#### **8. The City on Seven Hills (Revelation 17:9)**

**Prophetic Symbolism**:
- **Woman** = Church (Revelation 17:1-5 describes her as "the great harlot" - apostate church)
- **Seven mountains/hills** = Geographic identifier pointing to Rome
- **"Sits on"** = Located in, exercises authority from, dominates
- **"Great city which reigns"** = At the time of John's writing (~95 CE), Rome ruled the known world

**Revelation 17:9, 18**:
> "Here is the mind which has wisdom: **The seven heads are seven mountains on which the woman sits**... And the woman whom you saw **is that great city which reigns over the kings of the earth**." (Revelation 17:9, 18)

**Prophetic Identification: Rome/Vatican**

**The Seven Hills of Rome**:

| **Hill Name** | **Latin Name** | **Location** | **Significance** |
|--------------|---------------|-------------|-----------------|
| 1. **Aventine Hill** | Aventinus | Southern Rome | One of the original seven hills |
| 2. **Caelian Hill** | Caelius | Southeast Rome | Named after Etruscan warrior Caelius Vibenna |
| 3. **Capitoline Hill** | Capitolinus | Between Forum and Campus Martius | Most sacred hill, Temple of Jupiter |
| 4. **Esquiline Hill** | Esquilinus | Northeast Rome | Largest of the seven hills |
| 5. **Palatine Hill** | Palatinus | Central Rome | Birthplace of Rome, imperial residences |
| 6. **Quirinal Hill** | Quirinalis | North-central Rome | Named after god Quirinus |
| 7. **Viminal Hill** | Viminalis | Northeast of Quirinal | Smallest of the seven hills |

**Historical Context**:
- Rome has been called **"the city of seven hills"** (Latin: *Septem Montes*) since ancient times
- Classical writers (Virgil, Plutarch, Cicero) referenced Rome's seven hills
- **Vatican Hill** is adjacent to but not one of the original seven (located across the Tiber River)
- Vatican City sits within the boundaries of historic Rome, the famous city on seven hills

**Why This Identifies the Vatican**:

**Geographic Precision**:
- Only one major religious power headquarters is located in the city famous for seven hills: **Vatican City in Rome**
- No other major religious institution sits in "the city on seven hills"
- Fulfills the prophetic identifier with geographic specificity

**Historical Authority**:
- When John wrote Revelation (~95 CE), **Rome** was "that great city which reigns over the kings of the earth"
- Roman Empire dominated the known world politically and militarily
- Vatican continues this influence religiously and diplomatically

**Religious-Political Power**:
- **Woman** (church) sitting on **seven mountains** (Rome) = Religious power headquartered in Rome
- Vatican is the only religious entity that is simultaneously:
  * Located in historic Rome (city of seven hills)
  * Exercises authority as both church and state
  * Claims universal jurisdiction ("reigns over the kings of the earth" spiritually)
  * Maintains diplomatic relations with 180+ nations globally

**Connection to the Harlot (Revelation 17)**:

**Revelation 17:1-5** describes the woman:
> "Come, I will show you the judgment of **the great harlot who sits on many waters**, with whom the kings of the earth committed fornication... And on her forehead a name was written: **MYSTERY, BABYLON THE GREAT, THE MOTHER OF HARLOTS AND OF THE ABOMINATIONS OF THE EARTH**." (Revelation 17:1-2, 5)

**Characteristics Fulfilled**:

| **Prophetic Characteristic** | **Fulfillment in Vatican/Catholic Church** |
|----------------------------|------------------------------------------|
| **Sits on seven mountains (hills)** | Vatican located in Rome, the city on seven hills |
| **"Great city which reigns over kings"** | Vatican exercises religious-political influence over world leaders, diplomatic relations with 180+ nations |
| **Commits fornication with kings** | Church-state unions throughout history (Holy Roman Empire, concordats with nations) |
| **Dressed in purple and scarlet** (Rev 17:4) | Papal and cardinal vestments are purple and scarlet |
| **Adorned with gold, precious stones, pearls** (Rev 17:4) | Vatican's immense wealth, ornate churches, St. Peter's Basilica |
| **Golden cup full of abominations** (Rev 17:4) | Outward beauty hiding doctrinal corruption (changed Sabbath, added traditions and false teachings) |
| **"BABYLON THE GREAT"** (Rev 17:5) | Confusion - mixing pagan practices with Christianity (Sunday worship from sun god tradition) |
| **"Mother of harlots"** (Rev 17:5) | Protestant churches (daughters) retained Sunday observance despite leaving Catholic Church |
| **"Drunk with blood of the saints"** (Rev 17:6) | Inquisitions, martyrdom of Bible-believers, persecution of Sabbath-keepers |

**"Babylon" = Confusion**:
- Hebrew word *Babel* (Babylon) means **"confusion"**
- Describes religious system that confuses truth with error
- Mixes biblical teaching with pagan traditions (Sunday from sun worship, Easter from Ishtar, Christmas from Saturnalia, Immortal Soul, Purgatory, Idol worship)
- Elevates human tradition above God's commandments

**"Mother of Harlots"**:
- Catholic Church is the "mother" church
- Protestant churches are "daughter" churches (came out of Catholic Church during Reformation)
- Despite leaving Rome over indulgences and papal authority, Protestant churches **retained Sunday observance and other false teachings** (inherited from mother church)
- Thus they are called "harlots" - still in spiritual fornication with worldly powers through enforced Sunday worship

**The Seven Heads (Mountains) Explained**:

**Revelation 17:9-10**:
> "The seven heads are seven mountains on which the woman sits. There are also **seven kings**. Five have fallen, one is, and the other has not yet come."

**Dual Symbolism**:
1. **Seven Mountains** = Geographic identifier (Rome's seven hills)
2. **Seven Kings** = Two valid interpretations that both identify the same prophetic sequence:

**Interpretation 1: Seven Forms of Roman Government** (Traditional View):
   - Five fallen (before John's time): Kings, Consuls, Dictators, Decemvirs, Military Tribunes
   - One is (John's time): Imperial Rome (Caesars)
   - One to come: Papal Rome (arose after imperial Rome fell)

**Interpretation 2: Seven Prophetic World Powers** (Prophetic Sequence View):

This interpretation aligns perfectly with Daniel's four kingdoms prophecy and shows the complete sequence from Daniel's time to the end:

| **Kingdom/Power** | **Status in Revelation 17:10** | **Timeframe** | **Prophetic Significance** |
|------------------|-------------------------------|--------------|---------------------------|
| **1. Babylon** | "Five have fallen" | 605-539 BCE | First beast (Daniel 7:4); head of gold (Daniel 2:32, 38) |
| **2. Medo-Persia** | "Five have fallen" | 539-331 BCE | Second beast (Daniel 7:5); chest/arms of silver (Daniel 2:32, 39) |
| **3. Greece** | "Five have fallen" | 331-168 BCE | Third beast (Daniel 7:6); belly/thighs of bronze (Daniel 2:32, 39) |
| **4. Pagan Rome** | "Five have fallen" | 168 BCE-476 CE | Fourth beast (Daniel 7:7); legs of iron (Daniel 2:33, 40) |
| **5. Papal Rome** | "Five have fallen" | 538-1798 CE | Little horn (Daniel 7:8, 24-25); beast from sea (Rev 13:1-10); received deadly wound in 1798 |
| **6. Protestant USA** | **"One is"** (at time of enforcement) | 1776 CE-present | Beast from earth (Rev 13:11-18); **currently in power**, will enforce mark of beast |
| **7. Papal Rome Restored** | "Other has not yet come" | Future (when USA enforces papal authority) | Deadly wound healed (Rev 13:3); eighth king (Rev 17:11); restored to full authority when USA enforces Sunday laws |

**Key Insights on This Prophetic Interpretation**:

**"Five Have Fallen" (Past Powers)**:
- All five dominated God's people or the world stage in succession
- All five were world-ruling empires during their time
- All five passed away before the end-time scenario
- Papal Rome's first phase (538-1798) ended with deadly wound, making it part of the "fallen" sequence

**"One Is" (Current Power - Protestant USA)**:
- At the time when the mark is being enforced, Protestant USA is the dominant power
- Currently the world's superpower (military, economic, cultural influence)
- This is the beast from the earth (Revelation 13:11-18) in its active phase
- Will be the enforcing power that gives life to the image of the beast
- "One is" refers to the power **currently operating** when prophecy reaches climax

**"Other Has Not Yet Come" (Future Power - Papal Rome Restored)**:
- Papal Rome's deadly wound will be fully healed
- USA will enforce papal authority and Sunday laws globally
- Rome restored to full religious-political power it held 538-1798
- This is the "eighth king" (Revelation 17:11) that "is of the seven" (the fifth king - Papal Rome - restored)
- "When he comes, he must continue a short time" - brief final period of persecution before Christ's return

**Why This Interpretation Fits Perfectly**:

**1. Aligns with Daniel's Four Kingdoms**:
   - Daniel 2 and 7 establish Babylon → Persia → Greece → Rome sequence
   - Revelation continues where Daniel left off
   - Papal Rome is the continuation/transformation of the fourth kingdom (Rome)

**2. Matches the Beast's Identity**:
   - The woman (apostate church) sits on the beast (political powers)
   - The beast "was, and is not, and yet is" (Rev 17:8) = Papal Rome had power (538-1798), lost it (deadly wound), will have it again (wound healed)
   - Seven heads = Seven successive world powers that the apostate church influenced or rode

**3. Explains "The Eighth King"**:
   - **Revelation 17:11**: "The beast that was, and is not, is himself also the eighth, and is of the seven, and is going to perdition"
   - **The eighth** = Papal Rome in its final restored phase
   - **"Is of the seven"** = The eighth is the same as the seventh (Papal Rome restored), which was the fifth that "fell" (Papal Rome 538-1798)
   - Papal Rome appears **three times** in the sequence:
     * **5th king**: Papal Rome (538-1798) - "fallen" due to deadly wound
     * **7th king**: Papal Rome restored - "not yet come... continue a short time"
     * **8th king**: Same as 7th, emphasizing it's the final manifestation - "is of the seven, and is going to perdition"

**4. Explains Current Events**:
   - We are living in the time of the **sixth king** (Protestant USA)
   - Observing the preparation for the **seventh king** (Papal Rome restoration through USA enforcement)
   - Heritage Foundation Sunday rest advocacy = USA preparing to enforce papal authority
   - Vatican's growing diplomatic influence = deadly wound healing process
   - Sunday law movement = transition from sixth to seventh king beginning

**5. Matches Revelation 13's Sequence**:
   - **First beast** (Rev 13:1-10) = Papal Rome - received deadly wound (1798)
   - **Second beast** (Rev 13:11-18) = Protestant USA - gives life to image of first beast
   - **Wound healed** (Rev 13:3) = Papal Rome restored through USA's enforcement
   - Seven kings prophecy shows the **same sequence** from different angle

**The Prophetic Timeline**:

```
1. Babylon (fallen)
2. Persia (fallen)  
3. Greece (fallen)
4. Pagan Rome (fallen)
5. Papal Rome 538-1798 (fallen - deadly wound)
   ↓
   [Deadly Wound Period 1798-present]
   ↓
6. Protestant USA (currently "is" - the enforcing power)
   ↓
7. Papal Rome Restored (not yet come - when USA enforces)
   = 8th king (final manifestation, same as 7th)
   ↓
Christ Returns - Beast goes to perdition (Rev 17:11)
```

**Both Interpretations Valid**:

Both interpretations are biblically sound and identify the same core truth:
- **Traditional view**: Focuses on Rome's governmental forms, emphasizing continuity of Roman power
- **Prophetic sequence view**: Focuses on world-ruling powers in salvation history, emphasizing God's sovereignty over kingdoms

**The critical point both agree on**: Papal Rome is the final manifestation of the beast power, currently having its deadly wound healed, and will exercise brief but intense authority when Protestant America enforces its mark (Sunday law) globally.

**Revelation 17:11**:
> "The beast that was, and is not, is himself also **the eighth, and is of the seven**, and is going to perdition."

This verse confirms: The final power (eighth) is a restoration of one of the previous seven (Papal Rome - the fifth). It's the **same entity** in its ultimate form, which "was" (538-1798), "is not" (deadly wound 1798), and "yet is" (wound healing now, fully restored when USA enforces).

**Modern Application**:
The prophecy continues to be fulfilled:
- Vatican maintains headquarters in Rome (seven hills)
- Exercises global religious influence as predicted
- Diplomatic relations with most world governments
- Promoting Sunday rest globally (Economy of Francesco, European Sunday Alliance)
- Fulfilling role as religious-political power "reigning over kings"

**Why "Seven Hills" Matters**:
- **Precision**: Identifies Rome specifically (not Jerusalem, Mecca, or other religious centers)
- **Clarity**: Historical designation going back 2,500+ years
- **Fulfillment**: Vatican is the only major religious power headquartered there
- **Confirmation**: Adds to multiple identifying marks (changed law, persecuted saints, 1,260 years, etc.)

**The Complete Prophetic Picture**:

Daniel 7 + Revelation 13 + Revelation 17 = **Same Power**:
- **Daniel 7**: Little horn among ten kingdoms (European nations), changes times and law, persecutes 1,260 years
- **Revelation 13**: Beast from the sea (papacy), receives deadly wound 1798, wound heals, mark enforced
- **Revelation 17**: Woman (church) on seven hills (Rome), fornicates with kings, drunk with saints' blood

All three prophecies converge on the same entity: **The Roman Catholic Church/Vatican**, headquartered in Rome (the city on seven hills), exercising religious-political authority, changing God's law (Sabbath), and persecuting those who maintain biblical truth.

**Biblical Call**:

**Revelation 18:4**:
> "Come out of her, my people, lest you share in her sins, and lest you receive of her plagues."

God calls His people to recognize the system, reject its false teachings (especially Sunday sacredness), and return to biblical truth (seventh-day Sabbath). The identifying mark is clear: geographic (seven hills), historical (1,260 years), theological (changed law), and prophetic (all characteristics fulfilled).

### **The Iron and Clay Mixture (Daniel 2:41-43) - Modern Fulfillment**

Now that we've established the Vatican as the continuation of the fourth beast (Rome), we can see how Daniel 2's prophecy of iron and clay continues to be fulfilled today.

> "Whereas you saw the feet and toes, partly of potter's clay and partly of iron, **the kingdom shall be divided**; yet the strength of the iron shall be in it, just as you saw the iron mixed with ceramic clay. And as the toes of the feet were partly of iron and partly of clay, so the kingdom shall be partly strong and partly fragile. As you saw iron mixed with ceramic clay, **they will mingle with the seed of men; but they will not adhere to one another**, just as iron does not mix with clay." (Daniel 2:41-43)

#### **Interpretation of the Iron-Clay Mixture**

**IRON** = Roman political/military power continuing through **Roman Church authority (Vatican)**
- Roman legal system and governance structure preserved in Catholic Church canon law
- Vatican as continuation of Roman religious-political authority
- Papal claims to universal jurisdiction over all Christians
- Roman organizational hierarchy (pontiff, cardinals, bishops paralleling emperor, senate, governors)
- Latin language preserved as official church language

**CLAY** = The nations of Europe and modern nation-states
- Individual sovereign nations that emerged after Western Rome's fall (476 CE)
- France, Germany, Spain, England, Italy, Portugal, Netherlands, etc.
- Democratic governments and secular states
- National sovereignty and independence movements
- Separation of church and state principles

**IRON & CLAY MIXED** = Vatican influence within secular nations
- The Roman Church (iron) attempts to influence/control secular governments (clay)
- They "mingle" through concordats, treaties, and political influence
- They "will not adhere to one another" - unstable church-state relationships
- Sometimes cooperating (Catholic political parties, Vatican diplomacy)
- Sometimes in tension (secular laws vs. church doctrine)
- Church cannot fully control states; states cannot eliminate church influence

#### **Modern Examples of Iron-Clay Mixture**

**Mingling**:
- Vatican diplomatic relations with 180+ countries
- European Sunday Alliance (Vatican-backed pressure on EU nations)
- Economy of Francesco (Vatican influencing economic policy)
- Concordats between Vatican and nations (Italy, Germany, Spain, etc.)
- Catholic lobbying for Sunday laws in secular democracies
- Project 2025 (Catholic influence on U.S. policy)

**Not Adhering**:
- Nations maintain sovereignty despite Vatican pressure
- Secular laws override church preferences (abortion, divorce, same-sex marriage)
- Separation of church and state in most Western nations
- Failed attempts at theocracy in modern era
- Vatican's loss of Papal States (reduced to Vatican City in 1929)
- Limited enforcement power (must work through national governments)

**Connection to Sabbath Change**:
The Vatican (iron) mixed with secular nations (clay) attempting to enforce Sunday observance through civil law perfectly fulfills:
- Daniel 2:41-43 (iron-clay mixture that doesn't fully adhere)
- Daniel 7:25 (power that changes "times and law")
- Revelation 13:16-17 (mark of the beast enforced by legislation)

The Sabbath change from Saturday to Sunday represents the clearest evidence of this power's claim to authority above God's Word - and current Sunday rest initiatives suggest history is repeating itself.

### **The Wine of Babylon: False Doctrines**

**Revelation 17:2**:
> "With whom the kings of the earth committed fornication, and **the inhabitants of the earth were made drunk with the wine of her fornication**."

**Revelation 18:3**:
> "For all the nations have **drunk of the wine of the wrath of her fornication**, the kings of the earth have committed fornication with her."

**Biblical Symbolism of Wine in Prophecy**:

**Positive Context**:
- **Psalm 104:15**: "Wine that makes glad the heart of man" - blessing, joy, celebration
- **Matthew 26:27-29**: Blood of Christ, new covenant, communion

**Negative Context (Prophetic)**:
- **Wine** = False teachings, deceptive doctrines, spiritual intoxication
- **"Wine of fornication"** = False doctrines that seduce nations away from biblical truth
- **"Made drunk"** = Spiritually deceived, unable to discern truth from error
- **Effect**: Nations/people accept false teaching as truth (like alcohol impairs judgment)

**Jeremiah 51:7 - Old Testament Parallel**:
> "Babylon was a golden cup in the LORD's hand, that **made all the earth drunk**. The nations drank her wine; therefore **the nations are deranged**."

**Application to Revelation 17-18 (Modern Babylon)**:
- **Babylon (Catholic Church)** gives the world her "wine" (false doctrines)
- Nations and churches drink this wine, becoming spiritually intoxicated
- Unable to see biblical truth clearly because judgment is impaired by false teaching

#### **Jesus' Warning: The Doctrine of the Nicolaitans**

Before discussing the specific false doctrines of Babylon, it's crucial to understand that Jesus Himself warned against this very pattern in the early church:

**Revelation 2:6, 14-15**:
> "But this you have, that you **hate the deeds of the Nicolaitans, which I also hate**." (To the church in Ephesus)

> "But I have a few things against you, because you have there those who hold the **doctrine of Balaam**, who taught Balak to put a stumbling block before the children of Israel, to eat things sacrificed to idols and to commit sexual immorality. Thus you also have those who hold the **doctrine of the Nicolaitans, which thing I hate**." (To the church in Pergamos)

**Who Were the Nicolaitans?**

Historical evidence suggests the Nicolaitans were an early heretical sect known for:

1. **Compromising God's Law**: Teaching that since Christians are saved by grace, they can disregard God's commandments
2. **Cheapening Grace**: Using grace as license for sin rather than power to obey
3. **Incorporating Pagan Practices**: Mixing pagan customs and idolatrous practices with Christianity
4. **Sexual Immorality**: Tolerating fornication and idolatry under guise of Christian freedom

**The Connection to Balaam**:

Jesus links the Nicolaitans to **Balaam** (Numbers 22-25, 31:16), who:
- Couldn't curse Israel directly (God protected them)
- So taught Balak to corrupt Israel from within through compromise
- Led Israelites to mix worship of God with pagan idolatry (Baal of Peor)
- Introduced sexual immorality disguised as religious celebration
- Result: Israel weakened not by external attack but internal compromise

**Why Jesus Says "I HATE" This**:

This is one of the strongest statements in Scripture—Jesus rarely uses the word "hate," but He uses it **twice** regarding the Nicolaitans (Revelation 2:6, 15). Why?

- **Compromising God's law** destroys the foundation of relationship with Him
- **Cheapening grace** turns salvation into license for sin (Jude 4: "turning the grace of our God into lewdness")
- **Mixing paganism with Christianity** creates the very "Babylon" (confusion) God condemns
- **It destroys from within** what persecution couldn't destroy from without

**The Nicolaitan Pattern = Babylon's Pattern**:

| **Nicolaitan Characteristics** | **Babylon/Catholic Church Pattern** |
|-------------------------------|-------------------------------------|
| Compromising God's Law | Changed Sabbath (4th Commandment) to Sunday; removed 2nd commandment (graven images); altered 10th commandment |
| Cheapening Grace | Indulgences, purgatory, salvation through church sacraments rather than faith |
| Incorporating Pagan Practices | Sunday (sun worship), Christmas (Saturnalia), Easter (Ishtar), statues/images (idol worship), titles (Pontifex Maximus from paganism) |
| Sexual Immorality (spiritual) | Fornication with kings (church-state union); spiritual adultery (abandoning God's truth for human tradition) |
| Teaching Error | Papal authority to change God's law; tradition equal to Scripture; doctrines of demons |

**The Warning for Today**:

Just as Nicolaitans infiltrated the early church, **the same spirit operates today** in the Roman Catholic system and Protestant churches that retained Catholic traditions:

1. **Claim to follow Christ** while **changing His commandments** (Sunday for Sabbath)
2. **Speak of grace** while **teaching salvation through church authority/sacraments** 
3. **Mix pagan practices with Christianity** (Christmas, Easter, Sunday, images, titles)
4. **Call it "unity" and "progress"** while Jesus calls it **"which thing I hate"**

**Revelation 2:16** (Jesus' warning to Pergamos):
> "Repent, or else I will come to you quickly and will **fight against them with the sword of My mouth**."

The "sword of His mouth" is His Word (Hebrews 4:12; Ephesians 6:17). Jesus will **fight against** those who hold Nicolaitan/Balaam doctrines—mixing paganism with Christianity and compromising His law—by exposing them through Scripture.

**This document is that very sword**—using Scripture to expose:
- Sunday (pagan sun worship) mixed with Sabbath commandment
- Pagan philosophy (Trinity, immortal soul) mixed with biblical teaching
- Human tradition (papal authority) mixed with divine command
- Church-state union (fornication with kings) instead of separation

**The Nicolaitan spirit is the Babylon spirit**: Compromise, mixture, confusion, lawlessness disguised as Christianity.

**Jesus' verdict**: **"I HATE"** this doctrine (Revelation 2:6, 15).

#### **Babylon's Wine: Specific False Doctrines**

**Note**: Each doctrine listed below is examined in detail in Part III. See [Papal Authority](#papal-titles-and-biblical-blasphemy) and related sections for comprehensive biblical analysis.

| **False Doctrine ("Wine")** | **Biblical Truth** | **Effect of the "Wine"** |
|----------------------------|-------------------|------------------------|
| **Sunday sacredness** | Seventh-day (Saturday) Sabbath (Exodus 20:8-11) | Nations accept Constantine's change as Christian truth |
| **Trinity doctrine** | One God (Father), one Lord (Jesus Christ), Holy Spirit is their presence (1 Cor 8:6; Rom 8:9; John 14:18, 26) | Replaces biblical simplicity with Greek philosophy; obscures Father's supremacy |
| **Immortal soul** | Soul is mortal; immortality is conditional (Ezekiel 18:4, 20) | Enables belief in purgatory, eternal torment, immediate heaven/hell |
| **Eternal torment in hell** | Wicked ultimately destroyed, not tortured eternally (Malachi 4:1, 3) | Misrepresents God's character as cruel torturer |
| **Purgatory** | No biblical basis; conflicts with sufficiency of Christ's sacrifice | Justifies indulgences, prayers for the dead, papal authority |
| **Papal infallibility** | All humans fallible; Scripture alone is infallible (2 Timothy 3:16-17) | Elevates human authority above God's Word |
| **Tradition = Scripture** | Scripture alone is authority (Sola Scriptura) | Allows church to add/change doctrine at will |
| **Prayers to saints/Mary** | Pray directly to God through Christ alone (1 Timothy 2:5) | Creates mediators other than Jesus |
| **Transubstantiation** | Communion is memorial, not literal transformation (1 Corinthians 11:24-25) | Priest performs "miracle" giving him special power |
| **Infant baptism** | Baptism requires conscious faith and repentance (Acts 2:38) | Creates false security without personal conversion |
| **Salvation by works** | Salvation by grace through faith alone (Ephesians 2:8-9) | Keeps people in bondage to church system |

#### **The "Golden Cup" (Revelation 17:4) - How the Wine Is Served**

**Revelation 17:4**:
> "The woman was arrayed in purple and scarlet, and adorned with gold and precious stones and pearls, having in her hand **a golden cup full of abominations and the filthiness of her fornication**."

**Symbolism**:
- **Golden cup** = Outward beauty, attractive appearance, impressive ritual
- **Full of abominations** = Contents are corrupt despite beautiful container
- **Filthiness of fornication** = Spiritual adultery (false doctrine) hidden by beauty

**Application**:
- **Vatican's outward glory**: St. Peter's Basilica, magnificent cathedrals, elaborate vestments, solemn rituals
- **Beautiful liturgy**: Ancient traditions, impressive ceremonies, mystical atmosphere
- **But contents corrupt**: False doctrines (the wine) served in beautiful ceremony
- **Effect**: People attracted by beauty, swallow the poison without realizing

**Why the Cup Matters**:
The golden cup explains **how** false doctrine spreads so effectively:
- Beautiful packaging makes the poison palatable
- Impressive ceremony gives credibility to error
- Ancient tradition makes people trust without questioning
- The more attractive the cup, the less people examine the contents

#### **How the Wine Works: Spiritual Intoxication**

**Like Physical Intoxication**:
- **Impaired Judgment**: Cannot distinguish truth from error
- **False Confidence**: Feel spiritually secure while in deception
- **Dulled Conscience**: Accept practices that contradict Scripture
- **Dependency**: Rely on the system that intoxicated them (church authority)
- **Contagious**: Those intoxicated spread the deception to others

**Prophetic Description**:
- **"Made drunk"** (Revelation 17:2) - Past tense: Already happened throughout history
- **"Have drunk"** (Revelation 18:3) - Perfect tense: Ongoing effect continuing
- **"All nations"** - Global reach: Every nation influenced by these false doctrines

**The Deception Process**:
1. **Attraction** - Beautiful cup (impressive ceremony) draws attention
2. **Consumption** - Drink the wine (accept false doctrine as truth)
3. **Intoxication** - Judgment impaired (can't see biblical truth clearly)
4. **Dependency** - Rely on the system (trust church tradition over Scripture)
5. **Propagation** - Spread the wine (teach others the same false doctrines)

#### **Protestant Churches Drinking the Wine**

**Revelation 17:5**:
> "**MOTHER OF HARLOTS**"

**The Daughters (Protestant Churches)**:
- Came out of Catholic Church during Reformation (16th century)
- Rejected papal authority, purgatory, indulgences, salvation by works
- **BUT retained some of the "wine"** (false doctrines from mother church):
  - **Sunday observance** (biggest retention - continued enforcing Sunday as "Christian Sabbath")
  - **Immortal soul doctrine** (retained from Greek philosophy via Catholic theology)
  - **Eternal torment** (retained traditional view despite lack of biblical support)
  - **Infant baptism** (many Protestant denominations continue this practice)

**Why They're Called "Harlots"**:
- **Spiritual fornication** = Mixing truth with error, accepting tradition over Scripture
- Left mother church but kept some of her false teachings
- Especially Sunday worship - the mark of human authority over God's commandment
- Some now returning to church-state union (supporting Sunday laws)

**The Incomplete Reformation**:
- **What they rejected**: Papal supremacy, indulgences, purgatory, prayers to saints, transubstantiation
- **What they kept**: Sunday worship, immortal soul, eternal torment, infant baptism (in many cases)
- **The problem**: Kept drinking some of mother's wine while rejecting the golden cup itself
- **The result**: Still spiritually intoxicated on key doctrines (especially Sabbath)

#### **The Final Issue: Whose Authority?**

Now that we understand what the wine is (false doctrines), how it's served (golden cup), its effect (spiritual intoxication), and who drinks it (all nations including Protestant churches), we can see the central issue: **Whose authority will you follow?**

**God's Final Warning to the World - Revelation 14:6-12 (Three Angels' Messages)**:

**First Angel** (verse 7):
> "Fear God and give glory to Him, for the hour of His judgment has come; and **worship Him who made heaven and earth, the sea and springs of water**."
- Points to **Creator** and **Sabbath** (Exodus 20:11 uses same language as Creation week)
- Calls world back to worshiping Creator on His appointed day (seventh-day Sabbath)
- **Counter to the wine**: Reject human tradition, return to God's commandment

**Second Angel** (verse 8):
> "**Babylon is fallen, is fallen**, that great city, because she has made all nations **drink of the wine of the wrath of her fornication**."
- Announces Babylon's judgment
- Identifies her crime: Making nations drunk with false doctrine (the "wine")
- **Direct reference to the wine**: This is God's verdict on the intoxication system
- Includes Catholic Church and Protestant churches that retained her false teachings

**Third Angel** (verses 9-12):
> "If anyone worships the beast and his image, and receives his mark on his forehead or on his hand, he himself shall also drink of the wine of the wrath of God... Here is the patience of the saints; here are those who **keep the commandments of God** and the faith of Jesus."
- Warning against accepting the mark (enforced Sunday observance)
- Identifies God's people: Those who keep His commandments (including Sabbath) despite persecution
- **The sober choice**: Those who refuse the wine keep God's commandments

#### **Identifying God's Remnant Church: The Two Characteristics**

**Revelation 12:17** reveals the **two identifying marks** of God's true end-time church:

> "And the dragon was enraged with the woman, and he went to make war with **the rest of her offspring**, who **keep the commandments of God** and **have the testimony of Jesus Christ**."

**Two Non-Negotiable Characteristics**:

**1. Keep the Commandments of God**
- Not just acknowledge them, but **keep** them (obey them)
- All Ten Commandments, including the fourth (seventh-day Sabbath)
- No exceptions, no human authority to change them
- Exodus 20:8-11 still binding: "Remember the Sabbath day, to keep it holy... the seventh day is the Sabbath"

**2. Have the Testimony of Jesus Christ**

**What is "the testimony of Jesus"?** Scripture itself defines this:

> "And I fell at his feet to worship him. And he said unto me, See thou do it not: I am thy fellowservant, and of thy brethren **that have the testimony of Jesus**: worship God: **for the testimony of Jesus is the spirit of prophecy**." (Revelation 19:10)

**"The testimony of Jesus" = "The spirit of prophecy"**

This means God's remnant church will have:
- **The prophetic gift** (1 Corinthians 12:28; Ephesians 4:11-13)
- **Biblical prophecy understanding** (Daniel and Revelation correctly interpreted)
- **Modern prophetic guidance** (Joel 2:28-29 - Spirit poured out in last days)

#### **The Rare Combination: Why Most Churches Fail the Test**

**Almost All Churches Discuss Prophecy**:
- Catholic Church has eschatology teachings
- Protestant churches preach about end times
- Evangelical churches have prophecy conferences
- Pentecostal churches emphasize prophetic gifts

**But Almost None Do So Biblically**:

**Common Prophetic Errors**:
1. **Futurism** - Places antichrist in future, ignores 1,260 years of papal persecution already fulfilled
2. **Preterism** - Places all prophecy in past, denies current/future fulfillment
3. **Secret Rapture** - Not found in Scripture (see 1 Thessalonians 4:16-17 - Christ's return is loud, visible, global)
4. **Seven-Year Tribulation** - Misinterprets Daniel's 70 weeks (already fulfilled in Christ's time)
5. **Ignoring the Sabbath-Sunday issue** - Most prophecy teachers avoid identifying Sunday as mark of the beast
6. **Refusing to identify the papacy** - Political correctness prevents clear biblical identification of the antichrist system

**The Result**: 
- Churches claim to teach prophecy
- But avoid the **biblical conclusions** that would require them to change (leave Sunday, recognize papal system)
- They are **intoxicated** by Babylon's wine—unable to see clear prophetic truth

**God's Remnant Church Will**:
1. **Keep ALL God's commandments** - Including seventh-day Sabbath (not Sunday)
2. **Understand prophecy biblically** - Identify papal system, 1,260-year persecution, Sabbath-Sunday test, mark of the beast
3. **Have the spirit of prophecy** - Modern prophetic guidance warning of coming events
4. **Proclaim the Three Angels' Messages** - Call people out of Babylon before it's too late

**Revelation 14:12** (Third Angel's Message) **repeats** this two-fold identification:
> "Here is the patience of the saints; here are those who **keep the commandments of God** and **the faith of Jesus**."

**"The faith of Jesus"** = The testimony/message/truth that Jesus proclaimed, which includes:
- Keeping Father's commandments (John 14:15; 15:10)
- The prophetic word (Matthew 24; Luke 21; Revelation)
- Warning about false teachers and systems (Matthew 7:15-23)

#### **Why This Matters**

**The Dragon's Fury** (Revelation 12:17):
> "And the dragon was **enraged** with the woman, and he went to **make war** with the rest of her offspring..."

**Satan is enraged specifically at those who**:
1. **Keep God's commandments** (especially the Sabbath—the sign of allegiance to Creator, not tradition)
2. **Have the testimony of Jesus/spirit of prophecy** (understand and proclaim biblical prophecy, exposing Satan's deceptions)

**Why these two?**
- **Commandment-keeping** exposes the Sabbath-Sunday change and all of Babylon's false doctrines
- **Spirit of prophecy** gives clear understanding of Daniel/Revelation, identifying the beast system and calling people out

**Satan's strategy**: Get churches to either:
- Keep prophecy but **change the commandments** (Protestant churches: understand some prophecy but keep Sunday)
- Keep commandments but **ignore or misinterpret prophecy** (Some Sabbath-keeping groups that don't understand Daniel/Revelation clearly)
- **Reject both** (Most churches: changed commandments AND false prophetic interpretations)

**God's remnant will have BOTH**:
- **Commandments of God** (including unchanged Sabbath)
- **Testimony of Jesus** (spirit of prophecy—biblical understanding of end-time events and modern prophetic guidance)

**The Test is Now**: 
As you read this document, you are encountering **biblical prophecy** (testimony of Jesus/spirit of prophecy) that calls you to **keep God's commandments** (including Sabbath). This is precisely what Revelation 12:17 and 14:12 describe. The question is: Will you respond to this call, or will you remain intoxicated by Babylon's wine, unable to act on what Scripture clearly reveals?

**The Central Test**:
- **Babylon's wine** = Human tradition (Sunday, immortal soul, etc.)
- **God's truth** = Biblical commandments (seventh-day Sabbath, conditional immortality)
- **The question**: Will you follow tradition (wine) or Scripture (truth)?
- **The issue**: Whose authority do you accept—church tradition or God's Word?

**Why This Matters**:
The wine represents more than just false doctrines—it represents the **principle of human authority over divine authority**. When you accept Sunday (the wine), you accept the premise that church tradition can override God's commandment. When you reject the wine and return to Sabbath, you declare that God's Word alone is your authority.

#### **The Call to Come Out (Revelation 18:4-5)**

Having understood the wine (false doctrines), the cup (attractive packaging), the effect (intoxication), and the test (whose authority?), God issues His urgent call:

**Revelation 18:4-5**:
> "Come out of her, my people, lest you share in her sins, and lest you receive of her plagues. For her sins have reached to heaven, and God has remembered her iniquities."

**God's Warning**:
- **"My people"** - God still has faithful people within Babylon (Catholic and Protestant churches)
- **"Come out"** - Urgent call to separate from false doctrine (stop drinking the wine)
- **"Lest you share in her sins"** - Continuing in system makes you partaker of sins
- **"Receive of her plagues"** - Final judgments coming on Babylon system

**What "Coming Out" Means**:
1. **Reject false doctrines** - Stop accepting tradition over Scripture (spit out the wine)
2. **Return to biblical truth** - Especially seventh-day Sabbath vs. Sunday (choose God's authority)
3. **Refuse the mark** - Will not accept enforced Sunday observance (refuse the final intoxication)
4. **Follow Bible alone** - Sola Scriptura (Scripture as sole authority)
5. **Keep God's commandments** - Including fourth commandment Sabbath (remain sober with God's Word)

**Not Condemning People, But Calling Them Out**:
- God's call is **to His people** still within Babylon
- He loves them and wants them to escape the deception
- The call is not to leave sincere believers, but to leave the **system of false doctrine**
- Those who remain sober (reject the wine) will hear and respond

### **The Mark of the Beast vs. The Seal of God**

**Revelation 13:16-17**:
> "He causes all, both small and great, rich and poor, free and slave, to receive a mark on their right hand or on their foreheads, and that no one may buy or sell except one who has the mark or the name of the beast, or the number of his name."

**God's Seal** (Exodus 31:13-17; Ezekiel 20:12, 20):
- **The Sabbath**: Identifies God as Creator
- **Seventh-day observance**: Demonstrates loyalty to God's authority
- **Sign of sanctification**: "That you may know that I am the LORD who sanctifies you"
- **Biblical Foundation**: Fourth commandment (Exodus 20:8-11) - "Remember the Sabbath day, to keep it holy... the seventh day is the Sabbath of the LORD your God"

**Beast's Mark** (Revelation 13:16-17; 14:9-12):
- **Sunday observance**: Enforced by law
- **Human authority**: Demonstrates submission to tradition over Scripture
- **Sign of allegiance**: To church-state system rather than God
- **Historical Foundation**: Constantine's 321 CE Sunday law, Council of Laodicea Canon 29 (364 CE), Catholic Church admission of changing the Sabbath

**The Two Marks Contrasted**:

| **Aspect** | **God's Seal (Sabbath)** | **Beast's Mark (Sunday)** |
|-----------|------------------------|-------------------------|
| **Day** | Seventh day (Saturday) | First day (Sunday) |
| **Authority** | God's commandment (Exodus 20:8-11) | Human tradition (Constantine, Catholic Church) |
| **Biblical Basis** | Commanded by God, never changed | No biblical command, changed by man |
| **Identifies** | The Creator (Exodus 20:11) | The church-state system |
| **Loyalty** | To God above all | To human religious-political authority |
| **Result** | Eternal life with God | Second death (Revelation 14:9-11) |

**The Final Test**:
> "Here is the patience of the saints; here are those who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus." (Revelation 14:12)

The Sabbath becomes the visible test: Will you obey God's fourth commandment (seventh-day Sabbath) or submit to human tradition (Sunday) enforced by law?

**Forehead vs. Hand**:
- **Forehead** = Conscious choice, intellectual acceptance, genuine belief in Sunday sacredness
- **Hand** = Compliance for practical reasons (keep job, buy/sell, avoid persecution) despite knowing biblical truth

**When Does Sunday Become the Mark?**
Sunday observance becomes the "mark of the beast" when it is **enforced by law** and people must choose between:
1. **Obeying God** (keeping biblical seventh-day Sabbath) despite persecution
2. **Obeying human authority** (accepting mandated Sunday observance) to avoid consequences

Currently, Sunday observance is tradition - it becomes the "mark" when made compulsory through legislation with penalties for non-compliance.

- Even secular governments persuaded by "worker protection" argument

#### **Connection to Sabbath Change**

The **wine of Babylon** and the **Sabbath change** are inseparably connected:

**The Original Intoxication (321-538 CE)**:
1. Constantine offers the wine: "Day of the Sun" (321 CE) - sounds good, looks imperial
2. Church councils enforce it: Canon 29 of Laodicea (364 CE) - clothed in ecclesiastical authority
3. Nations drink: Roman Empire accepts Sunday (wine in golden cup of Roman power)
4. Effect: World becomes intoxicated, forgets biblical Sabbath

**The Continuing Intoxication (538-1798 CE)**:
- Papal supremacy enforces the wine: 1,260 years of Sunday observance
- Those who refuse the wine persecuted: Sabbath-keepers hunted, killed
- Nations remain drunk: Cannot see biblical truth about Sabbath

**The Modern Intoxication (1798-Present)**:
- Wine served in new cups: "Family values," "tradition," "environment"
- Protestant churches serve mother's wine: Sunday sacredness without papal authority
- Nations drink willingly: EU, Project 2025, global Sunday initiatives
- Preparing for final intoxication: Enforced Sunday law (mark of the beast)

**The Sobering Truth**:
- Only those who reject the wine will see clearly
- Only those sober with Scripture will recognize the deception
- Only those who "come out of Babylon" will escape the final delusion
- The test centers on Sabbath: God's seal vs. beast's mark

**Revelation 14:12**:
> "Here is the patience of the saints; here are those who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus."

Those who remain sober (reject the wine) will keep God's commandments - including the fourth, the seventh-day Sabbath - despite the world's intoxication with Sunday tradition.

## Understanding Babylon's Wine: The Pattern of Deception

**Before We Continue**: You've now seen the prophetic framework identifying the power that changed the Sabbath and the coming test of loyalty. But how does Babylon work? How does she deceive "all nations" (Revelation 18:3)?

**Babylon's Method - The Wine**:

Revelation describes Babylon holding a golden cup "full of abominations" (Rev 17:4) containing "wine" that makes "all nations drunk" (Rev 17:2; 18:3). This wine represents **false doctrines** - beautiful on the outside (golden cup, ancient tradition, impressive rituals) but spiritually poisonous within.

**The Pattern**: Babylon doesn't change just one doctrine. She systematically replaced biblical truth with human tradition across **multiple areas** - all during the same historical period (Constantine era, 300s-500s CE). Understanding this pattern helps us:

1. **Recognize the wine** in all its forms
2. **See the consistency** of substituting tradition for Scripture
3. **Understand why** the Sabbath change is part of a larger system of deception
4. **Identify which churches** have drunk Babylon's wine (including Protestant churches that retained some false teachings)

**What You'll See Next**: 

We'll examine **six major doctrines** Babylon changed during the Constantine era - the same period when she changed the Sabbath from Saturday to Sunday. Each follows the same pattern:

- ✓ **Biblical teaching** clearly stated in Scripture
- ✓ **Human tradition** introduced without biblical authority  
- ✓ **Constantine-era adoption** (300s-500s CE)
- ✓ **Protestant retention** (Reformation incomplete)
- ✓ **Part of "the wine"** deceiving nations

**The Six Doctrines** (besides Sabbath):
1. **[Papal Authority](#papal-titles-and-biblical-blasphemy)** - Exalting human authority above God's Word
2. **[State of the Dead](#the-state-of-the-dead-biblical-vs-catholic-vs-modern-christianity)** - Immortal soul vs. unconscious sleep
3. **[Hell](#what-hell-means-in-scripture)** - Eternal torment vs. final destruction  
4. **[The Soul](#what-the-bible-says-about-the-soul)** - Inherently immortal vs. mortal/conditional
5. **[The Mass](#the-mass-and-eucharist-biblical-teaching-vs-catholic-doctrine)** - Re-sacrifice of Christ vs. memorial of finished work
6. **[Trinity](#the-holy-spirit-biblical-teaching-vs-trinity-doctrine)** - Three co-equal persons vs. one God (Father) and His Son
7. **[Millennium/Rapture](#the-millennium-biblical-teaching)** - Various interpretations vs. clear biblical sequence

**Quick Navigation**: Each doctrine is examined in detail in Part III below. Click any doctrine name to jump to its section.

**Why This Matters**:

When we reach **Part IV: Contemporary Fulfillment**, you'll see how **ALL these doctrines converge** in the modern Sunday law movement:
- Religious authority (papal) claiming power to change God's law
- Environmental crisis framing (rest for Earth)
- Political coalition (Vatican + Protestant + Secular)
- Media normalization across denominations
- **The same wine, served in new cups**

**Keep the Main Issue in Focus**: 

While we examine these doctrines, remember: **the Sabbath remains the central test**. These other teachings show Babylon's pattern and help us recognize her wine - but the final issue will be **whose authority do we follow**: God's seventh-day Sabbath or man's first-day tradition?

As you read Part III, ask yourself: "Do I believe this because Scripture clearly teaches it, or because I simply inherited this tradition?" Many grew up in these systems—learning from parents, churches, and communities—never knowing anything different. The wine of Babylon has been passed down through generations, making it feel like truth simply because it's familiar. This prepares you to understand Part IV's urgency - these aren't ancient history lessons, they're showing you **how Babylon operates today**.
