**Isaiah 5:20**:
> "Woe to those who call evil good, and good evil; who put darkness for light, and light for darkness; who put bitter for sweet, and sweet for bitter!"

#### **The Sweet and Bitter Truth: A Prophetic Pattern**

There's a powerful symbolic pattern in Scripture that perfectly describes the experience of discovering biblical truth:

**Revelation 10:9-10**:
> "So I went to the angel and said to him, 'Give me the little book.' And he said to me, '**Take and eat it; and it will make your stomach bitter, but it will be as sweet as honey in your mouth**.' Then I took the little book out of the angel's hand and ate it, and **it was as sweet as honey in my mouth. But when I had eaten it, my stomach became bitter**."

**Ezekiel 3:1-3**:
> "Moreover He said to me, 'Son of man, eat what you find; eat this scroll, and go, speak to the house of Israel.' So I opened my mouth, and He caused me to eat that scroll. And He said to me, 'Son of man, feed your belly, and fill your stomach with this scroll that I give you.' So I ate, and **it was in my mouth like honey in sweetness**."

**The Meaning of Sweet Then Bitter**:

**1. SWEET IN THE MOUTH - Discovering Truth**:
- When you first hear biblical truth (like the seventh-day Sabbath, God's dietary laws, the mark of the beast prophecy), it's **sweet as honey**
- Excitement of discovery - "Finally, this makes sense!"
- Joy of understanding - "The Bible is consistent after all!"
- Hunger for more - "What else have I been missing?"
- The Word tastes good because it **is** good (Psalm 119:103: "How sweet are Your words to my taste, sweeter than honey to my mouth!")

**2. BITTER IN THE STOMACH - Internalizing What Truth Requires**:
- After you've learned the truth and **internalized what it requires from you**, it becomes **bitter**
- Realization: "This will cost me everything"
- Recognition: "I'll have to change my entire life"
- Understanding: "This will bring persecution, not acceptance"
- The truth becomes hard to digest when you count the cost:
  - Losing your job for keeping Saturday Sabbath
  - Losing friends/family who reject biblical truth
  - Being labeled "extremist," "fundamentalist," "cult member"
  - Giving up comfortable traditions and popular Christianity
  - Standing alone while everyone else follows the crowd

**Why This Matters Now**:

The same pattern applies to this entire document:
- **Sweet**: Learning that prophecy identifies the beast system, that God has a remnant people, that the Sabbath is Saturday
- **Bitter**: Realizing you must **act on this truth**—keep the Sabbath, warn others, face persecution, lose relationships and opportunities

**The Test of True Conversion**:
- Those who taste the sweetness but reject the bitterness → **Never truly internalized the truth** (heard it but didn't eat it)
- Those who swallow both sweet and bitter → **Genuine disciples** (ate the scroll completely, willing to obey regardless of cost)

**Jesus' Warning**:
> **Luke 14:26-33** - "If anyone comes to Me and does not hate his father and mother, wife and children, brothers and sisters, yes, and his own life also, he cannot be My disciple. And whoever does not bear his cross and come after Me cannot be My disciple... **So likewise, whoever of you does not forsake all that he has cannot be My disciple**."

The truth is sweet when you discover it. But it becomes bitter when you realize what it will cost you to follow it. **Both are necessary**—you must taste the sweetness to be drawn in, and you must swallow the bitterness to prove your commitment.

**The Question**: Have you only tasted the sweetness of this message, or have you swallowed the bitter reality of what obedience will cost?

**2 Timothy 3:12-13**:
> "Yes, and all who desire to live godly in Christ Jesus will suffer persecution. But evil men and impostors will grow worse and worse, deceiving and being deceived."

### The Guaranteed Persecution: A Biblical Promise, Not a Possibility

**The Scripture Doesn't Say "Maybe"**:

Notice the precise language of **2 Timothy 3:12**:
> "Yes, and **ALL** who desire to live godly in Christ Jesus **WILL** suffer persecution."

- Not "might suffer"
- Not "could face"
- Not "some will experience"
- **"ALL WILL"** - It's a **guarantee**, not a possibility

**The Modern Christianity Test**:

Here's a sobering observation that proves how far modern Christianity has drifted from biblical faith:

**If there's no persecution in your Christian life, you're not living godly in Christ Jesus according to Scripture.**

**The Evidence in Modern Christianity**:

Look at the current state of Christianity in Western nations (Europe, North America, Australia):
- **Millions of Catholics and Protestants** worshiping every Sunday
- **Massive churches** with thousands of members
- **Christian celebrities** widely accepted and celebrated
- **Prosperity gospel preachers** living in luxury
- **Contemporary worship** that mirrors secular entertainment
- **Watered-down sermons** that never offend anyone
- **"Seeker-friendly" services** designed not to challenge attendees

**The Question**: Where is the persecution Jesus promised? Where is the opposition Paul guaranteed?

**The Answer**: There isn't any—because they're not living godly lives that conflict with the world. They've compromised biblical standards to fit in.

**The Only Persecution Modern Christians Face**:

In regions where Christianity is dominant (USA, Europe, Australia), Christians rarely experience persecution **from other Christians**. The exception? Those who actually try to live biblically:

**Examples of What Brings Real Persecution Today**:

1. **Keep the Biblical Sabbath (Saturday)**:
   - Fired from jobs for refusing to work Saturdays
   - Mocked as "legalistic" or "Judaizers"
   - Called a "cult member" (Seventh-day Adventists face this constantly)
   - Excluded from mainstream Christian fellowship
   - See Patterson v. Walgreens case (2024) - fired for Sabbath observance

2. **Abstain from Alcohol**:
   - Ridiculed as "prudish" or "pharisaical"
   - Excluded from social gatherings centered on drinking
   - Labeled "judgmental" for not participating
   - Even Christian events now commonly serve alcohol

3. **Avoid Modern Entertainment** (violent movies, immoral TV shows, vulgar music):
   - Called "extreme," "out of touch," "legalistic"
   - Excluded from conversations about popular shows/movies
   - Viewed as "holier-than-thou"
   - Even Christians mock those who avoid worldly entertainment

4. **Dress Modestly** (biblical standards of modesty):
   - Ridiculed as "old-fashioned" or "oppressive"
   - Young people pressured to conform to immodest fashion
   - Churches no longer teach modesty standards
   - Those who maintain modesty are viewed as "extreme"

5. **Refuse to Work on Sabbath**:
   - Economic persecution (can't get certain jobs)
   - Career limitations (passed over for promotions)
   - Educational barriers (exams scheduled on Sabbath)
   - Social isolation (can't participate in Saturday activities)

6. **Speak Against False Doctrines** (Sunday sacredness, Trinity, immortal soul, eternal torment, papal authority):
   - Labeled "divisive," "fundamentalist," "cult member"
   - Excluded from ecumenical fellowship
   - Called "extremist" or "conspiracy theorist"
   - Accused of "causing disunity in the body of Christ"

7. **Take the Bible Literally** (creation in six days, biblical standards on marriage/gender, hell as destruction not eternal torture):
   - Mocked as "anti-science" or "ignorant"
   - Excluded from academic Christian circles
   - Called "dangerous" (see academic papers documented above)
   - Pope Francis calls this a "plague"

**The Pattern is Clear**:

The moment you actually start living according to biblical standards that conflict with:
- **Modern culture** (entertainment, dress, lifestyle)
- **Catholic tradition** (Sunday, Trinity, immortal soul)
- **Popular Christianity** (compromise, tolerance of sin, prosperity focus)

**You become the enemy**—not to the world primarily, but **to other Christians**.

**The Irony**:

- **Compromised Christianity**: No persecution, widespread acceptance, growing numbers, financial prosperity, cultural influence
- **Biblical Christianity**: Persecution, rejection, economic hardship, labeled "extremist/cult"

**Which one does Scripture promise will face persecution?**

**The Modern Test**:

If your Christianity is:
- ✓ Accepted by all denominations
- ✓ Approved by popular culture
- ✓ Celebrated by celebrities
- ✓ Praised by media
- ✓ Comfortable and convenient
- ✓ Never costs you anything (job, relationships, money)
- ✓ Doesn't require you to stand out as different

**Then according to 2 Timothy 3:12, you are NOT living godly in Christ Jesus**—because there's no persecution.

**The Biblical Test**:

True Christianity that follows Scripture **will** face persecution:
- ✗ **Sabbath-keeping**: Economic persecution, job loss, social exclusion
- ✗ **Biblical lifestyle**: Mocked as legalistic, pharisaical, extreme
- ✗ **Doctrinal purity**: Called divisive, fundamentalist, cult-like
- ✗ **Separation from world**: Ridiculed as backwards, out-of-touch
- ✗ **Taking Bible literally**: Labeled dangerous, anti-intellectual
- ✗ **Standing on biblical standards**: Accused of intolerance, hate

**Jesus' Words**:

> **John 15:18-20** - "If the world hates you, you know that it hated Me before it hated you. If you were of the world, the world would love its own. Yet **because you are not of the world, but I chose you out of the world, therefore the world hates you**. Remember the word that I said to you, 'A servant is not greater than his master.' **If they persecuted Me, they will also persecute you**. If they kept My word, they will keep yours also."

> **Matthew 5:10-12** - "Blessed are those who are persecuted for righteousness' sake, for theirs is the kingdom of heaven. **Blessed are you when they revile and persecute you, and say all kinds of evil against you falsely for My sake**. Rejoice and be exceedingly glad, for great is your reward in heaven, for so they persecuted the prophets who were before you."

> **Matthew 10:22** - "And you will be hated by all for My name's sake. But he who endures to the end will be saved."

> **Luke 6:22** - "Blessed are you when men hate you, and when they exclude you, and revile you, and cast out your name as evil, for the Son of Man's sake."

**The Uncomfortable Truth**:

Modern Christianity has made peace with the world—accepted Sunday (papal tradition), embraced prosperity gospel, watered down holiness standards, compromised with entertainment culture, abandoned biblical literalism—and therefore experiences no persecution.

**But the moment you return to biblical Christianity**:
- Keep Saturday Sabbath (God's command)
- Live holy, separated lifestyle (biblical standard)
- Reject false doctrines (papal traditions)
- Take Scripture literally (fundamental to faith)

**You will immediately experience what Jesus promised**: persecution, mockery, exclusion, economic hardship, being called "extremist" and "cult member."

**This persecution doesn't come primarily from atheists or other religions**—it comes from **compromised Christianity** that has drunk Babylon's wine and now views biblical obedience as fanaticism.

**The Proof**:

The fact that Sabbath-keepers face:
- Job discrimination (Patterson v. Walgreens, DOJ v. Lansing)
- Social ridicule (called "cult members")
- Religious exclusion (not accepted in ecumenical fellowship)
- Academic attack (called "fundamentalist plague")
- Papal condemnation (Pope Francis: fundamentalism is a "plague")

**Proves they are living godly in Christ Jesus**—because Scripture guarantees such persecution.

**The Mainstream Christian Experience**:

If you can attend Sunday church, watch any TV shows/movies, dress however you want, drink socially, never face job discrimination, be accepted by all denominations, and experience **zero persecution**—Scripture says you're not threatening Satan's kingdom.

**The Biblical Christian Experience**:

If you keep Saturday Sabbath, abstain from worldly entertainment, dress modestly, refuse alcohol, stand on biblical doctrine, and face **constant ridicule, job loss, and social exclusion**—Scripture says you're living godly in Christ Jesus, and this persecution is guaranteed.

**The Choice**:

- **Broad way**: Compromise Christianity that everyone accepts → No persecution (but Matthew 7:13 says leads to destruction)
- **Narrow way**: Biblical Christianity that costs everything → Guaranteed persecution (but Matthew 7:14 says leads to life)

**2 Timothy 3:12 is not a warning to be feared—it's a promise to be embraced**. If you're not being persecuted, you're not living godly enough to threaten the enemy. If you are being persecuted, rejoice—you're on the right path.

**The Strategy**:
1. **Redefine "fundamentalism"** from "following Scripture" to "dangerous extremism"
2. **Vilify obedience** as "intolerance," "divisiveness," "plague"
3. **Exalt interpretation** (by church/scholars) over plain biblical text
4. **Appeal to science/culture** to override God's Word
5. **Marginalize Bible-keepers** as "backwards," "unenlightened," "literalist"

### Why This Matters Now

**The Preparation for Sunday Law Enforcement**:

When Sunday laws are enforced (current initiatives documented in Part IV), those who refuse and keep Saturday Sabbath will be labeled:
- **Religious fundamentalists** (already called "plague" by Pope)
- **Divisive and intolerant** (refusing to unite around Sunday tradition)
- **Civil disobedients** (breaking Sunday rest laws)
- **Extremists** (taking Bible literally instead of accepting Catholic interpretation)
- **Threats to social order** (academic papers already calling biblical literalism "dangerous")

**The Groundwork is Being Laid**:
- Religious leaders call fundamentalism a "plague" → Prepares public to see Sabbath-keepers as threat
- Academics call literal Bible reading "dangerous" → Justifies legal action against those who follow Scripture
- "Intolerance" label attached to biblical obedience → Reframes persecution as protecting society from extremists

**Historical Parallel**:
- **Medieval**: "Heretics" (those following Bible) must be eliminated for society's good
- **Modern**: "Fundamentalists" (those following Bible) are plague/danger requiring legal restraint

### The Real Question

**Who is the villain?**

- Those who **follow what God wrote with His own finger** on stone tablets (Exodus 31:18)?
- Or those who **changed God's law by human authority** and now call obedience "extremism"?

**Who is divisive?**

- Those who **keep biblical Sabbath as Jesus did** (Luke 4:16)?
- Or those who **enforce human tradition** and label Scripture-followers as threats?

**Who is the fundamentalist?**

- Those who say **"Thus says the LORD"** and follow His commandments?
- Or those who say **"Thus says the Church"** and demand obedience to tradition over Scripture?

### The Biblical Response

**Acts 5:29**:
> "We ought to obey God rather than men."

**Matthew 15:3, 6-9**:
> "Why do you also transgress the commandment of God because of your tradition?... **Thus you have made the commandment of God of no effect by your tradition**. Hypocrites! Well did Isaiah prophesy about you, saying: 'These people draw near to Me with their mouth, and honor Me with their lips, but their heart is far from Me. And **in vain they worship Me, teaching as doctrines the commandments of men**.'"

**Revelation 14:12**:
> "Here is the patience of the saints; **here are those who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus**."

**The Call**:
When religious and academic authorities call you "fundamentalist," "extremist," "plague," or "divisive" for following God's Word—**rejoice**! You're in good company:

- **Jesus** was called divisive for keeping Sabbath and challenging tradition (John 7:12, 43; 9:16)
- **Apostles** were called troublemakers for preaching biblical truth (Acts 17:6)
- **Reformers** were called heretics for following Scripture over church authority
- **End-time saints** will be persecuted for keeping God's commandments (Revelation 12:17; 13:15-17)

**Matthew 5:10-12**:
> "Blessed are those who are persecuted for righteousness' sake, for theirs is the kingdom of heaven. Blessed are you when they revile and persecute you, and say all kinds of evil against you falsely for My sake. **Rejoice and be exceedingly glad, for great is your reward in heaven**, for so they persecuted the prophets who were before you."

## The Faithful Minority: A Pattern Throughout History

### "As in the Days of Noah"

Jesus Himself warned that His return would parallel the conditions of Noah's time:

> **Matthew 24:37-39** - "But as the days of Noah were, so also will the coming of the Son of Man be. For as in the days before the flood, they were eating and drinking, marrying and giving in marriage, until the day that Noah entered the ark, and did not know until the flood came and took them all away, so also will the coming of the Son of Man be."

> **Luke 17:26-27** - "And as it was in the days of Noah, so it will be also in the days of the Son of Man: They ate, they drank, they married wives, they were given in marriage, until the day that Noah entered the ark, and the flood came and destroyed them all."

**The Sobering Reality**: In Noah's day, only **eight people** were saved out of the entire world population.

> **1 Peter 3:20** - "...when once the Divine longsuffering waited in the days of Noah, while the ark was being prepared, in which **a few, that is, eight souls**, were saved through water."

> **2 Peter 2:5** - "And did not spare the ancient world, but **saved Noah, one of eight people**, a preacher of righteousness, bringing in the flood on the world of the ungodly."

**The Lesson**: 
- The entire world thought Noah was an extremist, a fundamentalist, a fanatic
- The majority mocked God's warning and continued in their traditions
- Only a tiny minority believed God and obeyed His command to enter the ark
- The majority perished despite their confidence, comfort, and numbers

### "As in the Days of Lot"

Jesus also compared the end times to Lot's era:

> **Luke 17:28-30** - "Likewise as it was also in the days of Lot: They ate, they drank, they bought, they sold, they planted, they built; but on the day that Lot went out of Sodom it rained fire and brimstone from heaven and destroyed them all. **Even so will it be in the day when the Son of Man is revealed**."

**The Sobering Reality**: In Sodom, only **Lot and his two daughters** were saved—and even Lot's wife perished because she looked back (Genesis 19:26).

> **Genesis 19:24-25** - "Then the LORD rained brimstone and fire on Sodom and Gomorrah, from the LORD out of the heavens. So He overthrew those cities, all the plain, all the inhabitants of the cities, and what grew on the ground."

**Only three people saved from entire cities**. Even Lot's sons-in-law thought he was joking when he warned them (Genesis 19:14).

**The Lesson**:
- The entire cities lived normally—business, commerce, building, planting
- Everyone thought Lot was overreacting to God's warning
- Only a tiny minority believed God's warning and escaped
- Even among those warned, some chose comfort over obedience (Lot's wife, his sons-in-law)

### The Pattern Throughout Scripture: The Faithful Minority

**Throughout biblical history, God's faithful people have always been the minority**:

**Elijah's Time**:
> **1 Kings 19:14, 18** - Elijah said: "I alone am left; and they seek to take my life." But God said: "Yet I have reserved seven thousand in Israel, all whose knees have not bowed to Baal, and every mouth that has not kissed him."

**Isaiah's Time**:
> **Isaiah 1:9** - "Unless the LORD of hosts had left to us a very **small remnant**, we would have become like Sodom, we would have been made like Gomorrah."

**Jesus' Own Warning**:
> **Matthew 7:13-14** - "Enter by the narrow gate; for **wide is the gate and broad is the way that leads to destruction, and there are many who go in by it**. Because **narrow is the gate and difficult is the way which leads to life, and there are few who find it**."

**Key Words**:
- **Wide gate / Broad way** = MANY go this way → **destruction**
- **Narrow gate / Difficult way** = **FEW** find it → **life**

> **Luke 13:23-24** - Then one said to Him, "Lord, are there **few who are saved**?" And He said to them, "**Strive to enter through the narrow gate, for many, I say to you, will seek to enter and will not be able**."

**The Question Jesus Will Ask**:

> **Luke 18:8** - "Nevertheless, when the Son of Man comes, **will He really find faith on the earth**?"

This is a rhetorical question expecting the answer: **Very little**. Jesus is warning that when He returns, genuine biblical faith will be rare—most will have accepted traditions over truth.

### The Final Generation: Sunday Keepers vs. Sabbath Keepers

**Apply this to the Sabbath/Sunday question**:

**Current Religious Statistics (2025 Verified Data)**:

**Sunday Keepers** (observing human tradition):
- **Catholic Church**: 1.3+ billion
- **Protestant denominations** (keeping Catholic Sunday): 900+ million
  - Baptist, Methodist, Presbyterian, Lutheran, Anglican/Episcopal, Pentecostal, Non-denominational, etc.
- **Total Sunday keepers**: **2.2+ billion Christians**

**Saturday Sabbath Keepers** (following biblical commandment):

| **Group** | **Members** | **Key Facts** |
|-----------|-------------|---------------|
| **Seventh-day Adventists** | **23,684,237** | GC Annual Statistical Report, Dec 31, 2024; present in 200+ countries |
| **Ethiopian Orthodox Tewahedo Church** | **60,000,000+** | Largest single Christian body observing Saturday; never adopted Roman Sunday shift |
| **Eastern Orthodox Churches** | 230,000,000+ | Never legislated against Saturday; Synod of Trullo (692 AD) explicitly rebuked Rome for fasting on Saturday — still honor it as Sabbath alongside Sunday worship |
| **Seventh Day Baptists** | **70,000** | Oldest Protestant Saturday tradition; founded 1650, England; now in 17 countries |
| **Church of God (Seventh Day)** | ~200,000 | Multiple bodies tracing roots to Adventist / Miller movement |
| **Independent Messianic Jewish communities** | **350,000–1,000,000** | Fastest-growing via direct Bible study and social media; many without denomination |
| **Independent African & Asian Saturday movements** | **Millions** | Fastest-growing region globally; arrive at Saturday independently through Bible reading alone |
| **WCG/Armstrong splinter bodies** | **~30,000+** | UCG (~17,000), Living Church of God (~10,000), and 50+ other groups — see below |

**The WCG/Armstrong Test Case — What Happens When Sunday Is Imposed**:

Herbert Armstrong founded the Radio Church of God (1934), renamed Worldwide Church of God (WCG, 1968). The WCG was a strictly Saturday-keeping body with 150,000+ members at its peak. After Armstrong's death (January 16, 1986), his successor Joseph Tkach Sr. progressively dismantled Sabbatarian doctrine. In December 1994, Tkach formally announced the shift to Sunday observance.

**The result was immediate and decisive**: Approximately two-thirds of all WCG members walked out rather than abandon Saturday Sabbath. They formed 50+ independent Saturday-keeping fellowships — the largest being United Church of God (~17,000) and Living Church of God (~10,000). The WCG itself, now renamed Grace Communion International (GCI, 2009), retained only a fraction of its former membership.

**The prophetic lesson**: When Sunday is officially imposed on people who know the biblical truth of Saturday, the majority choose Saturday at personal cost. This is a preview of the end-time test.

**Protestant Leaders Who Admitted Sunday Has No Biblical Authority**:
- **Martin Luther**: *"There is no word of God that has prescribed the Lord's Day. Sunday is not a matter of faith."*
- **John Calvin**: Struggled to provide a clear biblical basis for Sunday vs. Saturday in the *Institutes*
- **Charles Spurgeon**: Acknowledged the Sabbath commandment specifies the seventh day
- **[See full collection: 60 Protestant Denominational Statements](#protestant-churches-admissions-on-sunday-observance)**

**The Fastest-Growing Sabbath Movement**:

Independent African, Asian, and Messianic communities are independently arriving at Saturday observance through direct Bible reading — repeating the exact Reformation pattern (*sola scriptura* applied without institutional gatekeeping). Social media is accelerating this process globally. The Saturday-keeping community is growing while mainstream Christianity declines in the West.

**Total Saturday Sabbath Keepers (Conservative Estimate)**: **90–110 million** (Ethiopian Orthodox alone = 60M+)

**The Ratio Corrected**: 
- **Sunday keepers**: ~2,200,000,000
- **Saturday Sabbath keepers**: ~90,000,000–110,000,000
- **Ratio**: Approximately **20 to 1** (not 100 to 1 as previously estimated when Ethiopian Orthodox was omitted)

**Still a minority — but a far larger one than most realize. And it is growing.**

**For every one person keeping the biblical seventh-day Sabbath, approximately 20 are keeping the papal Sunday tradition.**

### "Will He Find Faith?"

**The parallel is striking**:

| **Historical Event** | **Faithful Minority** | **Unbelieving Majority** | **Result** |
|---------------------|----------------------|-------------------------|-----------|
| **Noah's Flood** | 8 people (Noah's family) | Entire world population | Only 8 saved |
| **Sodom & Gomorrah** | 3 people (Lot, 2 daughters) | All inhabitants of cities | Only 3 saved |
| **Elijah's Era** | 7,000 faithful | Majority worshiping Baal | Only remnant saved |
| **Jesus' Warning** | "Few" finding narrow gate | "Many" on broad way to destruction | Few saved |
| **End-Time Sabbath** | ~90–110 million Saturday-keepers | ~2.2 billion Sunday-keepers | ? |

**The Question for Reflection**:

Throughout history, has the **majority** ever been right when it contradicted God's clear command?

- Majority rejected Noah's message → **perished in flood**
- Majority rejected Lot's warning → **destroyed by fire**
- Majority worshiped Baal instead of God → **only remnant saved**
- Jesus said majority take broad way → **leads to destruction**
- Today, majority keep Sunday despite no biblical authority → **?**

### The Comfort of Numbers vs. The Call to Obedience

**The Human Tendency**: We find comfort in numbers. "Billions can't be wrong!" 

**But Scripture warns**:

> **Exodus 23:2** - "You shall **not follow a crowd to do evil**; nor shall you testify in a dispute so as to turn aside after many to pervert justice."

> **Matthew 7:21-23** - "Not everyone who says to Me, 'Lord, Lord,' shall enter the kingdom of heaven, but he who does the will of My Father in heaven. **Many will say to Me in that day**, 'Lord, Lord, have we not prophesied in Your name, cast out demons in Your name, and done many wonders in Your name?' And then I will declare to them, '**I never knew you; depart from Me, you who practice lawlessness!**'"

**Notice**: Jesus says "**MANY** will say to Me in that day"—not a few, but MANY professing Christians will be shocked to hear "I never knew you."

**Why?** Because they practiced "lawlessness" (Greek: *anomia* = without law, breaking God's law).

**The Connection**:
- They called Jesus "Lord" → Religious, sincere
- They prophesied, cast out demons, did wonders → Active in ministry
- They were confident of salvation → Expected Jesus to accept them
- **But they practiced "lawlessness"** → Breaking God's commandments
- Jesus declares: **"I never knew you"**

**Application**: Millions of sincere Christians keep Sunday (breaking the fourth commandment) while being confident in their salvation. They are active in church, do good works, call Jesus "Lord"—yet they follow human tradition over God's clear command.

Will Jesus say to them: "You practiced lawlessness—you broke My Father's Sabbath commandment and followed human tradition instead"?

### The Critical Difference: Noah Was Right Because God Said So

**Why was Noah right and the world wrong?**
- Not because he was in the majority (he wasn't—8 vs. billions)
- Not because his message was popular (it wasn't—he was mocked)
- Not because it made logical sense (building an ark for rain no one had seen)
- **Because God commanded it, and Noah obeyed**

**Why was Lot right and Sodom wrong?**
- Not because most people agreed with him (they didn't)
- Not because his lifestyle was celebrated (he was considered extreme)
- Not because leaving was convenient (he lost everything)
- **Because God commanded it, and Lot obeyed**

**Why are Sabbath-keepers right and Sunday-keepers wrong?**
- Not because they are the majority (they're 1% of Christians)
- Not because it's popular (it brings ridicule and discrimination)
- Not because it's convenient (Sabbath-keeping costs jobs, educational opportunities, social acceptance)
- **Because God commanded the seventh-day Sabbath, and He never changed it**

### The Final Test: Will You Follow the Crowd or Follow God?

**When Sunday laws are enforced (see Part IV: Contemporary Fulfillment)**:

**The Broad Way** (majority):
- "Everyone is keeping Sunday—2.2 billion Christians can't be wrong!"
- "The Pope, all the churches, the government say Sunday is right"
- "If I don't comply, I'll lose my job, can't buy or sell, face persecution"
- "Surely God understands I have to provide for my family"
- **This is the wide gate and broad way → destruction**

**The Narrow Way** (minority):
- "God said 'Remember the Sabbath day'—He wrote it with His own finger"
- "Jesus kept the seventh-day Sabbath—I will follow His example"
- "Catholic and Protestant sources admit Sunday has no biblical authority"
- "I will obey God rather than men, regardless of consequences"
- **This is the narrow gate and difficult way → life**

### "As It Was in the Days of Noah"—So Shall It Be

**In Noah's day**:
- People lived normal lives: eating, drinking, marrying, building
- They had their religious traditions and felt spiritually secure
- They mocked Noah's "extreme" message about coming judgment
- They were confident the majority couldn't be wrong
- **Then suddenly**: "The flood came and took them all away" (Matthew 24:39)

**In the last days**:
- People will live normal lives: working, worshiping, doing good deeds
- They will have their religious traditions (Sunday) and feel spiritually secure
- They will mock "fundamentalists" who insist on biblical seventh-day Sabbath
- They will be confident that billions of Christians can't be wrong
- **Then suddenly**: "So also will the coming of the Son of Man be" (Matthew 24:39)

**Hebrews 11:7** - "By faith **Noah**, being divinely warned of things not yet seen, moved with godly fear, **prepared an ark for the saving of his household, by which he condemned the world** and became heir of the righteousness which is according to faith."

**Notice**:
- Noah was "divinely warned" → God told him what was coming
- He "condemned the world" by his obedience → His actions showed the world's disobedience
- He became "heir of righteousness" → Saved because he believed and obeyed

**Today, Sabbath-keepers are "divinely warned"**:
- God's Word clearly commands seventh-day Sabbath
- Biblical prophecy warns Sunday enforcement is coming (Revelation 13-14)
- By keeping God's Sabbath, they "condemn" the world's tradition
- They will become "heirs of righteousness"—saved because they believed and obeyed

### The Sobering Conclusion

**Jesus Himself warned**: When He returns, it will be **like Noah's day** and **like Lot's day**.

**In both cases**:
- The majority perished
- Only a tiny minority was saved
- The saved minority were those who **believed God's warning** and **obeyed His command** despite mockery, pressure, and isolation

**Today**:
- 2.2 billion Christians keep Sunday (no biblical authority)
- 22 million Christians keep biblical Sabbath (clear biblical command)
- **100 to 1 ratio** against God's commandment

**Jesus' question haunts us**: "When the Son of Man comes, will He really find faith on the earth?" (Luke 18:8)

**Faith means**:
- Believing what God said (Sabbath is the seventh day)
- Obeying what God commanded (Keep the Sabbath holy)
- Trusting God despite the majority (Following Jesus' example, not human tradition)
- Standing firm when tested (Refusing the mark of the beast—enforced Sunday law)

### The Choice Before Every Reader

**You must decide**:

**Will you trust**:
- The **majority** (2.2 billion Sunday-keepers) following human tradition?
- Or the **Word of God** (biblical Sabbath) even if you're in the tiny minority?

**Will you believe**:
- "Billions of Christians can't be wrong about Sunday"?
- Or "God's Word never changes, and He said the seventh day is the Sabbath"?

**Will you follow**:
- The **crowd** (wide gate, broad way) because it feels safe?
- Or **Jesus** (narrow gate, difficult way) because He is truth?

**Remember**:
- In Noah's day, **billions** were wrong, and **eight** were right
- In Lot's day, **entire cities** were wrong, and **three** were right
- In the last days, Jesus asks: "Will He find faith?"

**The answer depends on whether you will stand with the faithful minority who obey God's commandments, or join the majority who follow human tradition—even when that tradition contradicts the clear Word of God written with His own finger on tables of stone.**

> **Revelation 14:12** - "Here is the patience of the saints; **here are those who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus**."

> **Revelation 22:14** - "**Blessed are those who do His commandments**, that they may have the right to the tree of life, and may enter through the gates into the city."

**The faithful minority will be saved. The question is: Will you be among them?**

### Final Appeal

> "Come out of her, my people, lest you share in her sins, and lest you receive of her plagues." (Revelation 18:4)

> "Truly, these times of ignorance God overlooked, but now commands all men everywhere to repent, because He has appointed a day on which He will judge the world in righteousness by the Man whom He has ordained. He has given assurance of this to all by raising Him from the dead." (Acts 17:30-31)

**God no longer accepts ignorance as an excuse**. The evidence has been presented. The truth is available. Catholic and Protestant sources alike admit Sunday observance has no biblical authority. The historical record is clear. The prophecies point unmistakably to these times. Now God commands repentance—a return to His truth—because He has appointed a day of judgment.

God has faithful people in every denomination—Catholic, Protestant, and non-denominational. He calls them to:

1. **Study Scripture** for themselves (Acts 17:11 - Bereans searched Scriptures daily)
2. **Test traditions** against biblical teaching (1 Thessalonians 5:21 - Test all things)
3. **Reject false doctrines** (Babylon's wine) no matter how attractive the presentation
4. **Return to biblical truth** including the seventh-day Sabbath, biblical understanding of God the Father and His Son, proper understanding of the Holy Spirit, Christ's one sacrifice finished at the cross (not re-sacrificed in Mass), death, hell, soul, and Christ's return
5. **Prepare for persecution** that will come when standing for truth—no secret rapture escape
6. **Trust in Jesus** who saves by grace and empowers obedience
7. **Understand the times** recognizing we are living in final events before Christ's visible, glorious return

**The 7-day week has remained stable throughout all history**—an enduring testimony to Creation week. The seventh-day Sabbath remains as God established it, waiting for His people to return to His rest.

**The time is short**. Current initiatives (Vatican Sunday lobbying, Project 2025, EU pressure) show the final events are rapidly approaching. The choice each person makes—God's commandments or human tradition—will determine their eternal destiny.

> "If you love Me, keep My commandments." (John 14:15)

The question is not whether we can explain away the Sabbath through theological arguments, but whether we will obey what God clearly commanded and never changed.

**May God give each reader wisdom, courage, and grace to stand for truth regardless of the cost.**

## Conclusion

This comprehensive study reveals a consistent pattern of human authority superseding divine command across multiple doctrinal areas—all originating in the same historical period and advancing toward a prophetic climax.

### The Central Issue: Whose Authority?

The fundamental question underlying every topic in this document is: **Will we follow God's Word or human tradition?**

> "We ought to obey God rather than men." (Acts 5:29)

> "In vain they worship Me, teaching as doctrines the commandments of men." (Matthew 15:9)

### Questions for Reflection

1. **Authority**: If the Sabbath was established at creation (Genesis 2:2-3), commanded by God (Exodus 20:8-11), observed by Jesus and apostles, and never changed by biblical authority—on what basis do we accept a human-instituted change?

2. **Consistency**: If we accept Sunday based on tradition despite lack of biblical authority, what prevents accepting other traditions that contradict Scripture?

3. **Prophetic Fulfillment**: Given the precise fulfillment of biblical prophecy (four empires, 1,260 years exact to the year, seven hills geographic identification)—should we take seriously the warnings about future enforcement of Sunday observance?

4. **The Wine**: Have we been spiritually intoxicated by Babylon's wine (false doctrines) so that we cannot discern biblical truth from human tradition?

5. **Coming Out**: If God calls His people to "come out of Babylon" (Revelation 18:4), what does that mean practically? Must we reject all false doctrines, including Sunday observance, to escape the coming judgments?

6. **Modern Repetition**: Are we witnessing Constantine's Sunday law repeated in modern form—using secular justifications (family values, environment, worker rights) to enforce religious tradition?

7. **The Mark**: When Sunday observance becomes legally enforced (as current initiatives suggest is coming), will we have the courage to stand for biblical truth despite economic hardship and persecution?

8. **Protestant Dilemma**: If Protestant churches rejected papal authority but retained Sunday observance (a purely papal change with no biblical basis), have they truly separated from Rome?

9. **Millennium Understanding**: Does believing we're currently in the millennium (amillennialism) or expecting to escape tribulation (secret rapture) affect our readiness for persecution and understanding of God's final judgment?

10. **Christ's Return**: If Jesus said "every eye will see Him" and He'll come with "great sound of a trumpet," why do millions expect a secret, silent rapture?

11. **Trinity Doctrine**: If Scripture identifies "one God, the Father" (1 Corinthians 8:6) and "one Lord Jesus Christ," and the Holy Spirit is called the "Spirit of God" and "Spirit of Christ" interchangeably (Romans 8:9)—on what biblical basis do we believe in three co-equal divine persons? Why does Jesus say "My Father is greater than I" (John 14:28) if they are co-equal?

12. **Marriage Analogy**: If Scripture says husband and wife "become one flesh" (Genesis 2:24) while remaining two distinct persons, why do we reject this same concept when Jesus says "I and My Father are one" (John 10:30)—interpreting it as metaphysical Trinity rather than unified relationship?

13. **The Mass and "It Is Finished"**: When Jesus cried "**It is finished**" (John 19:30) and Scripture says He offered "**one sacrifice for sins forever**" (Hebrews 10:12), how can the Catholic Mass be a true re-presentation of Christ's sacrifice? If Christ's work is complete, why would He need to be offered again—even "in an unbloody manner"—at every Mass? Does celebrating Mass honor Christ's finished work or deny its sufficiency?

### The Call to Decision

This document presents extensive evidence showing:
- **Biblical teaching** on multiple topics (Sabbath, nature of God and Holy Spirit, state of dead, hell, soul, Mass/Eucharist, millennium, Christ's return)
- **Historical changes** made by human authority during Constantine era (Sabbath to Sunday, biblical God to Trinity, simple memorial to re-sacrifice Mass, conscious death to immortal soul)
- **Prophetic fulfillment** with remarkable precision (Daniel, Revelation)
- **Current convergence** toward enforced Sunday observance (2024-2026)
- **Catholic admissions** (39 official statements) acknowledging the Church changed the Sabbath by its own authority
- **Protestant admissions** (60 denominational statements) acknowledging Sunday has no biblical basis—virtually every major Protestant denomination
- **Final warning** (Three Angels' Messages, call to come out of Babylon)
- **End-time clarity** on millennium and Christ's visible, glorious return

**The choice before each person**:

> "Choose for yourselves this day whom you will serve... But as for me and my house, we will serve the LORD." (Joshua 24:15)

Will we:
- **Follow God's Word** (seventh-day Sabbath, one God the Father and His Son, Christ's one sacrifice "once for all", biblical doctrines) despite persecution?
- **Or follow human tradition** (Sunday, Trinity, re-sacrifice of Christ in Mass, immortal soul) for social/economic convenience?

The Sabbath becomes the **visible test**:
- Those who keep God's commandments (including fourth - Sabbath) show loyalty to Creator
- Those who accept human tradition (Sunday) show submission to earthly authority
- **Both Catholic and Protestant sources admit** Sunday has no biblical warrant—yet most continue observing it

**Revelation 14:12** describes God's faithful people:
> "Here is the patience of the saints; here are those who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus."

### The Gospel Hope

While this document exposes error and warns of coming persecution, the ultimate message is **hope through Jesus Christ**:

**Salvation by Grace**:
> "For by grace you have been saved through faith, and that not of yourselves; it is the gift of God, not of works, lest anyone should boast." (Ephesians 2:8-9)

- We are saved by Christ's sacrifice, not by Sabbath-keeping or any other work
- However, those who love Jesus will obey His commandments (John 14:15)
- The Sabbath is not a means of salvation but a sign of loyalty to the Savior

> "If you love Me, keep My commandments." (John 14:15)

> "Now by this we know that we know Him, if we keep His commandments. He who says, 'I know Him,' and does not keep His commandments, is a liar, and the truth is not in him. But whoever keeps His word, truly the love of God is perfected in him." (1 John 2:3-5)

> "Blessed are those who do His commandments, that they may have the right to the tree of life, and may enter through the gates into the city." (Revelation 22:14)

> "And whatever we ask we receive from Him, because we keep His commandments and do those things that are pleasing in His sight." (1 John 3:22)

> "Here is the patience of the saints; here are those who keep the commandments of God and the faith of Jesus." (Revelation 14:12)

**The Promise**: God doesn't demand obedience to burden us but to **bless** us. Those who keep His commandments have:
- **Access to the tree of life** (Revelation 22:14)
- **Answers to prayer** (1 John 3:22)

- **Joy in His house of prayer** (Isaiah 56:7)
- **Delight in the LORD** (Isaiah 58:14)
- **A sign of relationship** with God (Ezekiel 20:12, 20)

Obedience flows from love, not fear. We keep the Sabbath not to earn salvation but because we love the Savior who saved us by grace.

**God's Character Vindicated**:
- Eternal torment doctrine misrepresents God as cruel torturer
- Biblical teaching shows God is just: wicked are destroyed, not tortured forever
- God's law (including Sabbath) reflects His character: love, rest, freedom

**Final Victory Promised**:
> "He will wipe away every tear from their eyes; there shall be no more death, nor sorrow, nor crying. There shall be no more pain, for the former things have passed away." (Revelation 21:4)

Those who remain faithful through the final test will receive eternal life in the new earth, where God's Sabbath will be kept forever (Isaiah 66:22-23).

### Understanding the Basics

**Biblical Sabbath**: Friday sunset to Saturday sunset (Genesis 1:5, Leviticus 23:32)

> **Exodus 20:8-11** - "Remember the Sabbath day, to keep it holy. Six days you shall labor and do all your work, but the seventh day is the Sabbath of the LORD your God..."

**What it means**:
- ✅ Worship, prayer, Scripture study
- ✅ Rest from work and secular concerns  
- ✅ Fellowship with believers
- ✅ Quality time with family
- ✅ Nature, acts of mercy, spiritual focus
- ❌ Regular employment, shopping, secular entertainment, unnecessary work

> **Isaiah 58:13-14** - "Call the Sabbath a delight, the holy day of the LORD honorable... then you shall delight yourself in the LORD."

God designed the Sabbath as **"a delight,"** not a burden.

**Note on Prophetic Interpretation**:
This document represents the historicist school of biblical prophecy interpretation, which views prophetic fulfillment as occurring throughout history from the prophet's time to the end of the age. This approach has been held by many Protestant Reformers and continues in various denominations today. Readers are encouraged to study these topics personally, comparing all teachings with Scripture (Acts 17:11), and seeking guidance from the Holy Spirit (John 16:13). Alternative interpretive approaches (preterist, futurist, idealist) exist and reach different conclusions about prophetic fulfillment. The millennium and rapture teachings presented follow plain biblical reading rather than symbolic reinterpretation (amillennialism) or recent inventions (secret pre-tribulation rapture).

**Important Historical Context**: The majority of these alternative interpretation methods (preterist, futurist, idealist) were developed by Jesuit scholars as part of the Counter-Reformation—essentially an arm of Rome designed to deflect Protestant identification of the papacy as the Antichrist. The historicist method, which clearly identifies the papal system as the little horn of Daniel 7 and the beast of Revelation 13, was universally held by Protestant Reformers. In response, Jesuit theologians Francisco Ribera (late 1500s) developed futurism (pushing Antichrist to a future individual), and Jesuit Luis de Alcasar developed preterism (pushing Antichrist to the past—Nero or ancient Rome), both designed to remove suspicion from the papal system. These Jesuit counter-interpretations have, tragically, been widely adopted by Protestant churches today, effectively neutralizing the Reformers' prophetic witness against the papacy.

**Additional Counter-Reformation Doctrines**: Beyond prophetic interpretation methods, other teachings that deviate from plain biblical reading also emerged or were reinforced during similar periods:

- **Amillennialism**: Introduced by Augustine (~400 CE) during the Constantine era when the church gained political power and claimed to be the kingdom rather than waiting for Christ's literal return. This symbolic reinterpretation of Revelation 20's clear six references to "thousand years" parallels the same era that changed Sabbath to Sunday, introduced the immortal soul doctrine, and established eternal torment teaching—all moving from literal biblical reading to symbolic/philosophical interpretation favoring church authority.

- **Secret Pre-Tribulation Rapture**: Invented by John Nelson Darby in the 1830s (Plymouth Brethren) and popularized through the Scofield Reference Bible (1909), Hal Lindsey's *The Late Great Planet Earth* (1970), and the *Left Behind* series (1995-2007). This teaching, unknown to the early church and contradicting all biblical descriptions of Christ's visible, loud return that destroys the wicked, has become dominant in evangelical Protestantism. It requires belief in the immortal soul doctrine and promotes a secret "escape" rather than biblical preparation for standing firm through persecution.

- **Idealist Interpretation**: While less defined in origin than preterism and futurism, the idealist approach treats Revelation as timeless spiritual principles rather than historical fulfillment, similarly deflecting attention from identifying the papal system as the prophetic antichrist power.

All these methods share a common pattern: they move away from plain, literal biblical reading toward interpretations that either enhance church authority (amillennialism, Catholic origin) or neutralize prophetic warnings about apostate church power (Jesuit futurism, preterism, idealism; Darby's rapture theory). The result is that modern Protestantism, having largely abandoned historicist interpretation, cannot recognize the fulfillment of biblical prophecy happening in their own time—particularly regarding Sunday law enforcement as the mark of the beast.

### The Watchman's Responsibility: Why You Must Share This Truth

Many who discover these biblical truths ask: "Isn't it enough that I know? Do I really need to tell others?" The Bible answers clearly: **We have a sacred responsibility to warn those we love.**

### God's Command to the Watchman

> **Ezekiel 3:17-19** - "Son of man, I have made you a **watchman** for the house of Israel; therefore hear a word from My mouth, and give them warning from Me: When I say to the wicked, 'You shall surely die,' and you give him no warning, nor speak to warn the wicked from his wicked way, to save his life, that same wicked man shall die in his iniquity; **but his blood I will require at your hand**. Yet, if you warn the wicked, and he does not turn from his wickedness, nor from his wicked way, he shall die in his iniquity; **but you have delivered your soul**."

**Key Points:**
- God appoints believers as **watchmen** - those who see danger and must warn others
- If we see the truth but remain silent, God holds us **accountable** for those who perish in ignorance
- If we warn and they reject it, we've fulfilled our responsibility—**their choice is between them and God**

### The Watchman's Job: Warning of Danger

> **Ezekiel 33:6** - "But if the watchman sees the sword coming and **does not blow the trumpet**, and the people are not warned, and the sword comes and takes any person from among them, he is taken away in his iniquity; **but his blood I will require at the watchman's hand**."

**What This Means:**
- The **"sword"** = Coming judgment (Sunday law enforcement, persecution, final crisis)
- The **"trumpet"** = Warning message (sharing biblical truth about Sabbath, Babylon's wine, etc.)
- **"Blood at the watchman's hand"** = God holds us responsible if we stay silent

**We are not responsible for their decision—but we ARE responsible to warn them.**

### The New Testament Confirmation: Paul's Watchman Example

> **Acts 20:26-27** - "Therefore I testify to you this day that **I am innocent of the blood of all men**. For I have not shunned to declare to you **the whole counsel of God**."

**Paul's Defense:**
- He warned everyone—Jew and Gentile, popular and unpopular truths
- He declared the **whole counsel of God**, not just comfortable doctrines
- Because he faithfully warned, he is **"innocent of the blood of all men"**

**Application:** If Paul needed to warn people to be "innocent of blood," so do we. Silence is not an option.

### The Warning Must Be Clear and Urgent

> **Isaiah 58:1** - "**Cry aloud, spare not; lift up your voice like a trumpet**; tell My people their transgression, and the house of Jacob their sins."

**God's Command:**
- **"Cry aloud"** - Don't whisper, don't hint—proclaim boldly
- **"Spare not"** - Don't hold back out of fear of offense
- **"Like a trumpet"** - Loud, clear, unmistakable warning
- **"Tell My people"** - Even believers need to hear truth they've missed

**This isn't about being harsh—it's about loving people enough to tell them the truth even when it's uncomfortable.**

### Love Requires Warning

> **Proverbs 27:6** - "Faithful are the wounds of a friend, but the kisses of an enemy are deceitful."

**The Principle:**
- A **true friend** tells you hard truths that may sting but save your life
- An **enemy** (or coward) flatters you and lets you walk into danger
- **Love warns**; indifference stays silent

**If you saw your neighbor's house on fire, would you:**
- Stay silent because "it's not my place to tell them what to do"?
- Whisper politely so you don't offend them?
- **Or shout loudly to wake them up before they perish?**

**The Sabbath truth is a spiritual "house fire." Sunday law enforcement is coming. People need to be warned NOW.**

### The Eternal Consequences of Silence

> **James 4:17** - "Therefore, to him who knows to do good and does not do it, **to him it is sin**."

**Application:**
- You now **know** the biblical Sabbath truth
- You **know** Sunday observance has no biblical authority
- You **know** persecution is coming for those who keep God's commandments
- **If you stay silent, James says it's sin**

> **Jude 1:22-23** - "And on some have compassion, making a distinction; but others **save with fear, pulling them out of the fire**, hating even the garment defiled by the flesh."

**Jude's Urgency:**
- Some people need gentle compassion

### You Are Not Alone in This Responsibility

### Historical Documents

**Early Church Writings**:
- Epistle of Barnabas (~130 CE) - First known text arguing for Sunday replacing Sabbath
- Justin Martyr, First Apology (~150 CE) - Description of Sunday worship
- Eusebius, Ecclesiastical History - Records of early Christian practices
- Sozomen, Ecclesiastical History - Documentation of Constantine's Sunday law

**Church Councils**:
- Council of Nicaea (325 CE) - Canons and decrees, separation from Jewish practices
- Council of Laodicea, Canon 29 (363-364 CE) - "Christians must not Judaize by resting on the Sabbath"
  - Source: Hefele, Charles Joseph. *A History of the Councils of the Church*

**Imperial Edicts**:
- Constantine's Sunday Law (321 CE) - Codex Justinianus 3.12.2
  - Text: "On the venerable Day of the Sun let the magistrates and people residing in cities rest"
  - Source: *Codex Theodosianus* and *Codex Justinianus*

**Protestant Reformation Documents - Identification of Papacy as Antichrist**:

**Reformers' Writings**:
1. **Martin Luther** (1483-1546):
   - *Against the Roman Papacy, an Institution of the Devil* (1545)

   - Numerous sermons and writings identifying papacy as Antichrist

2. **John Calvin** (1509-1564):
   - *Institutes of the Christian Religion* (1536, multiple editions)
   - Commentary on 2 Thessalonians
   - *Treatises Against the Anabaptists and Against the Libertines*

3. **John Knox** (1505-1572):
   - *The First Blast of the Trumpet Against the Monstrous Regiment of Women*
   - Various tracts on papal tyranny

4. **Thomas Cranmer** (1489-1556):
   - *Defence of the True and Catholic Doctrine of the Sacrament*
   - Writings on papal authority and biblical prophecy

5. **Philipp Melanchthon** (1497-1560):
   - *Treatise on the Power and Primacy of the Pope* (1537)
   - Various theological works on papal claims

**Protestant Confessions of Faith**:

1. **Westminster Confession of Faith** (1646):
   - **Chapter 25, Section 6**: "There is no other head of the Church but the Lord Jesus Christ. Nor can the Pope of Rome, in any sense, be head thereof; but is that Antichrist, that man of sin, and son of perdition, that exalts himself, in the Church, against Christ and all that is called God."
   - Still official doctrine for Presbyterian and Reformed churches worldwide
   - Available online: https://www.pcaac.org/bco/westminster-confession/

2. **London Baptist Confession** (1677/1689):
   - **Chapter 26, Section 4**: Identical language to Westminster—identifies pope as "that antichrist, that man of sin, and son of perdition"
   - Still official doctrine for many Baptist churches
   - Also known as Second London Baptist Confession

3. **Smalcald Articles** (1537):
   - Written by Martin Luther
   - Part of Lutheran *Book of Concord* (1580)
   - **Part II, Article IV**: "The Pope is the very Antichrist, who has exalted himself above, and opposed himself against Christ"
   - Still official Lutheran confessional standard

4. **Thirty-Nine Articles of Religion** (1563):
   - Anglican/Episcopal standard
   - While less explicit, Anglican theology and homilies historically identified papacy as Antichrist
   - Available in *Book of Common Prayer*

5. **Augsburg Confession** (1530):
   - Foundational Lutheran confession
   - References to papal authority and Antichrist
   - Written by Philipp Melanchthon, approved by Martin Luther

**Secondary Historical Sources on Reformation**:
- D'Aubigné, J.H. Merle. *History of the Reformation*. Multiple volumes. (Documents reformers' views)
- Foxe, John. *Foxe's Book of Martyrs* (1563). (Protestant martyrs under papal persecution)
- Various historical compilations of Reformation writings
